<Author>Chriswith2kidsandawife
<Content>Good value, great staff, lots of steps! The Magic Castle hotel is good value - we booked 2 rooms which were really large suites, with a kitchenette, sofabed and large dining table. This would make an ideal base for staying for a few days to explore LA.Pros:- Good value- Close to Graumann's Chinese Theatre etc.- Great staff (really, they were very helpful and cheerful)- Free mini bar; saves a fortune on candy and soda for the kids and water for us.- great complementary continenal breakfast- pool open all hoursCons:- Lots and lots of stairs. A bit of a pain when dragging in 2 week's worth of luggage into and out of, but other than that not a problem.- No views from the rooms- could do with the interior decor updating and brighter lighting in the rooms (they were really quite dark even in full daylight)We stayed just around the corner from the Magic Castle hotel, in the Hollywood Celebrity , in March. Whilst their rooms are cheaper, they are also smaller and there is no pool.As long as you aren't expecting the Ritz, this is a great place to stay.

<Author>Phil2408
<Content>Excelletn value in the heart of Hollywood The Magic Castle is an excellent hotel, particularly well suited to families, just a few minutes walk from Hollywood Boulevard, Chinese Theatre, Walk of Fame etc. The suites are very large - plenty of room for families. However, they are quite old - the bathroom and kitchen fittings are particular dated, so if you are looking for a modern luxury hotel, this might not be for you. But even so, this hotel offers fantastic value with excellent service in a great location with lots of nice touches. On arrival, you are given a glass of lemonade and there is a turndown service with chocolates left on your pillow. But best of all is the free mini-bar. Unlimited soft drinks and candy all day. It really is free. At the prices usually charged for cola, this is a big money saver. The continental breakfast is very nice, and there is a good pool. The staff are excellent - they will help you will anything you ask them.

<Author>nthsh01
<Content>Great Service-Great Location-A LIttle Shabby Spent one night at the Magic Castle, at the beginning of a week long vacation in Southern California. Our flight arrived at LAX an hour early, so we were concerned about arriving too early in the morning at the hotel. Not to worry, we not only received a friendly greeting and the obligatory fizzy lemonade in a champagne flute, but we were told our room was ready, and we were upgraded to a two bedroom suite. That was quite a pleasant surprise, but I guess after reading all the plaudits here for their service, it shouldn't be so suprising at all.The suite was obviously an old 1930's apartment, with some great architectual details - a living room, kitchen, huge bathroom, and two big bedrooms. Closets galore, and some really great toiletries. The furnishings, paint, etc. could use an upgrade, they were a bit shabby, and there was an odd smell in the entire suite. Several of the obviously new plantation shutters had some damage, which was a shame, as they looked great.The continental breakfast in the morning was much appreciated - nothing special, but very convenient. And the free snacks, soda, water, etc. at any time are a great plus.Combine all that with the suberb location, right next to the famous Magic Castle and you've got a winner. A bit faded, perhaps, but we'd stay again, for sure. Great staff, great location.

<Author>vdams
<Content>magic castle a big hit with family My husband, our two teenage children and I spent four nights at the castle and enjoyed it very much. We checked right in (did not get the welcome drink everyone talks about and I saw others get when they checked in) to a bottom floor room facing the pool that I had requested when I booked directly with the hotel. We like the room right away because of the size ( we just came from a much smaller room in san fran.) My son was in his glory with the free snacks that were given to him with a smile every time. I also made use of this feature on beach days and we must of saved a good one hundred bucks overall getting snacks before we left for the day. We swam one night the pool was clean and heated with nice music playing. We loved the baked goods in the morning the best of any continental breakfast we ever had. Another great feature of the hotel is they have washer and dryers. we were on vacation for two weeks so we need to do some wash. washer was one dollar per load and dryer around seventy five cents. They give you free laundry detergent. This hotel is everything this web site claims it to be. Friendly hard working staff, clean, great location , and with All the freebies its a good value for families. I have to give a shout out to the housekeeping staff. perfect service never knocking on door when we slept in and room always spotless when we returned with the extra turn down service you don't see much any more in this class hotel. Now I do have one complaint and its pretty significant. the air conditioning system is old and very loud which made it hard for me to get a good nights rest. Besides the noise the room temp changed from hot to cold all night long blankets on blankets off. I was unable to get up as early as I usually do making my mornings a little rushed. I never complained about this to management because moving rooms was not an option for me ( I hate doing that more then anything) and I read that was a problem so I suspected all the rooms were like that. I know the manager reads this site. Please do something with the air conditioners and you will have your self a perfect hotel in my opinion. Thanks for a great time.

<Author>JENSBritinCopenhagen
<Content>If only... Hotels in LA are not cheap, so to find a property in this location whch offers this much space with these facilities and this level of service is a real find.  We, a family of four, stayed in a 1 bedroomed apartment for four days in mid July and we were allocated room 210 which is located at the back of the hotel with a balcony with a view over the pool. There was plenty of space for us all, and plenty of cupboard space as well. For your dollar you get a large double bedroom, a large living room with sofa bed, a kitchenette with space for four people to sit and eat and a bathroom with all the nececessaries. Continental breakfast, which you collect in reception and eat either in your room, balcony or beside the pool, is included in the price, there is covered car parking available at $10 per day, a very cosy pool/courtyard area and free snacks and soft drinks all day. If you want to stay in the middle of the Hollywood action, the location is perfect, just a few minutes walk from Hollywood/Highland. There are drawbacks, however. There is no lift and we saw plenty of people struggling with their cases up and down the stairs, although we were lucky enough to have a staff member help us on checking in. Do NOT expect luxury furniture and fittings - our bathroom had screw holes in the wall and mould around the bath partition. Finally, the outdoor walkways to and between the rooms are dimly lit and not particularly clean - although the rooms themselves are absolutely fine. What makes this place the top rated hotel in LA is the service. I have stayed in many hotels in many countires and I have never experienced a better standard of service. All the staff managed to hit exactly the right combination of friendliness and efficiency. Nothing was too much trouble. We were given directions to the subway, recommendations of where to eat, what to see and even how to tip.They gave us free passes to the nearby LA Fitness facility and a lift up to the wonderful Yamashiro restaurant further up the hill. They booked us tickets for the Magic Castle and insisted on driving us the 100 meters to the front door because my wife was wearing high heels. All the staff deserve the high praise you can read in these reviews. Truely exceptional. As I mention earlier, there are a few cons and if you are a couple looking for a luxury break or on business looking for business facilities, then the MCH may not be for you. For everybody else I would highly recommend this hotel. If only they could tidy up the bathrooms and walkways.....  
<Date>Aug 12, 2008

<Author>Smooth_Sluggo
<Content>Great staff, but overrated ranking This hotel is a great example of how different types of hotels appeal to different types of people. If you are a family with lots of kids who would sacrifice room quality for quantity (size), the Magic Castle is perfect for you. If you don't have kids, you may be disappointed in the quality of the rooms.The staff at the Magic Castle is the best I have ever seen in the US. They go out of their way to smile, assist, and otherwise be polite. As an example, I asked for directions to NBC studios, and they promptly looked up the best route on mapquest.com, and gave me the printout, while concurrently advising me of the best / worst times to drive. Unlike other hotels that have a good staff, at the Magic Castle they seem very sincere. They deserve the oft-mentioned recognition. However, there is one downside: the check-in counter is very narrow (as is the front entrance), so they can only serve one person at a time...when they try to accommodate 2 guests, it becomes quite chaotic. The location is also excellent. Its one long block off of Hollywood Blvd, so its easy to walk there. The room comes with free WiFi and the 'free mini-bar' was also a nice touch. The breakfast may not fill up some people, but I was personally happy with it. I had a suite and the room was huge--much more than my wife and I needed. It would be great for kids. Unfortunately, the bathroom was very small, with peeling paint and tiles and an unintentional retro look of the 70's. The beds, carpeting, and furniture looked like it was several decades old, though the bedding was excellent and the downturn service--complete with tomorrow's temperature and soft music on the new stereo--was very nice. Sadly, it seems lost on the tiny TV and cheap (thin and harsh) towels...the plusses and the minuses cancel each other out. There was one other major disappointment with this room. The first was noise. It may be far enough from Hollywood Blvd to not hear anything there, but if you're on the ground floor with a room on Franklin Ave, good luck trying to sleep unless you turn up the tiny AC unit and drown everything out with white noise. Trucks seem to rumble on Franklin all night long, and you can hear every footstep in the room above you. I would have switched rooms but I also knew the hotel was full during my stay, so I didn't bother. As comfortable as the bedding was, it was hard to sleep with all the racket.If my wife and I return with our kids, we would definitely stay here again--there's lots of room for them to run around, and the cheapness of the room will alleviate any fears of their misbehavior. Based on this scenario, I could see them as being the best that LA has to offer. But would I return without them? I am sorry, but I could not recommend it. And having stayed in several other hotels in LA before, I can't quite fathom how its #1 overall. Respectfully submitted.  
<Date>Aug 7, 2008

<Content>Great surprise!! We stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel while we were in L.A. recently and I was thoroughly impressed with the staff and the service they were second to none. It is in a great location too, just one street away from Hollywood Blvd. I would recommend this hotel with no hesitation please don't be put off with the basic furniture in the living area everything else more than makes up for that. <Author>travelluvr
<Content>Awesome staff We stayed at the Magic Caste Hotel on a recent side-trip to a family reunion. We arrived early and unfortunately were not able to check in. That was fine as we had just travelled from NY and were starving. They sent us to The Grill for lunch and said they would call when the room was ready. We walked around the corner to the the Hollywood/Highland Complex and had lunch. The front desk called within an hour to tell us the room was ready. I had asked to be put on a waiting list for a 2 bedroom but there weren't any available. They offered to move us if we wanted the next day when one became available. The thought of packing up again didn't appeal to us so we stayed put! The room was fine- very clean and spacious with plenty of space to have 4 people spread out. We had 2 yound adult kids with us- 18  20. The 20 yr old got the sleeper sofa and the daughter shared the 2 queen beds with us in the bedroom. The bathroom was small but certainly adequate and it was nice to be able to open the window as there wasn't a fan. The 2nd day we returned hot and exhausted to our room at 4:30 and it hadn't been cleaned yet. The cleaning staff was just entering it when we got to the hotel. We were a little disappointed but just got a drink and waited on the pool deck with the free snacks. The parking garage is really different- you need 2 people to operate the entry system and it is very tight quarters. We never used the pool- it was closed the day we arrived -very milky white. The following 2 days people swam in it and it looked fine. Again ,everything around us was very clean. The 3rd day I asked if we could take the bath towels withus to the beach. Before I knew it - the girl at the front desk had packed us up a beach bag with beach towels, snacks and cold water. She even wanted to give us sunscreen!! This service is what MCH is all about. There wasn't anything they wouldn't do to make your stay wonderful. The location is perfect for Hollywood in a very safe residential neighborhood. My only concern was when we checked out there were 2 calls from our room which we never made. We had cell phones and honestly never even saw the room phone. Also- there was no one in LA for us to call! It was a local # and I would bet that housekeeping probably used the phone. That was the day we were at the beach the whole day. We paid the $2 fee and that was the end of it. It could use a coat of paint to spruce things up but other than that- it was great and we would return. There is nowhere else in LA you can stay for the price. The breakfast was fantastic and my kids loved it. The snacks came in handy and we even walked around the corner to Longs and bought a bottle of wine! I would highly recommend MCH.

<Author>drbabbers
<Content>Pure Magic!! Check InWe arrived at the hotel at 10am, this wasn鈥檛 an issue at all as our room was ready for us. The check in was a very friendly and welcoming experience; I was given a glass of complimentary lemonade and also an overview to the local area. I was also informed of the complimentary 24/7 mini bar! My initial impressions after the check in were very positive.HotelThe room itself was not a suite, but a king bed. The bed was very comfortable and it actually has a proper duvet as opposed to a single sheet that is very common in hotels. The bathroom was also nice, particularly the shower which was a large walk in style with sliding doors. The stairway leading up to our hotel could have done with a paint job and a bit of an update, but a minor complaint in such a fantastic place. Also provided was a large LCD and DVD player. Don鈥檛 forget to ask for a free DVD rental at reception! They have a large selection of complimentary DVD鈥檚 that you can watch in your room. Overall the room was average looking and could probably do with an update, but it was adequate for our needs and we felt very comfortable. Glancing round the hotel, the suites look very cool! We also had a fridge freezer in our room, but no other kitchen facilities, useful for keeping our drinks in and that was about it.There is a well sized heated swimming pool in the centre of the hotel, which is an attractive feature to glance at when you walk through the reception area. The rooms are kind of built surrounding it and if you are lucky you will have a balcony overlooking the pool. The hotel also has a very secure and cosy feeling to it when you are roaming about.Breakfast is also included and is a very relaxing and fulfilling experience. They have a continental breakfast on display which was very satisfying. We relaxed by the pool enjoying our food with other guests, everyone seemed to be very happy and this created a positive atmosphere for your morning meal. A great start to the day!Another thing worth mentioning is the free mini bar they offer. You can go to the front desk and ask for anything off the menu for free. It is a good selection of snacks and drinks, very impressive and served to you with a smile always.The free wireless internet access was the only real upset here. It was a working service, but was very slow pretty much every day. It was useable, but not as fast as other hotels I have stayed in.It is also worth mentioning that as the hotel is small and cosy, the noise can sometimes be a bit frustrating. The main thing is slamming doors. Pretty much every morning I could hear doors slamming at early hours, I guess some people are just inconsiderate to others. Some hotel have devices on the doors to prevent them slamming, something the Magic Castle may want to invest in perhaps.Staff100 percent the best hotel staff I have ever experienced. All of the staff at the Magic Castle are exceptional and provide the best service in any hotel I have stayed in. They all deserve a pay rise and are the backbone to this hotel. Every single person I spoke to was extremely helpful and also happy to listen to what I had to say. They also demonstrated going that extra mile on many occasions, Example 1: Myself and my partner were relaxing by the pool when one of the staff approached us offering us bottled water or a popsicle!, perfect to quench us whilst bathing in the hot sun. Example 2: I went to the front desk and asked for a DVD for the evening, the lady then said 鈥榟ow about some popcorn to go with that?鈥?I actually didn鈥檛 have a microwave in my room, but don鈥檛 worry they then offered to microwave it for me and bring it to our room! 2 minutes later there was a knock on the door and we had our delicious popcorn ready to eat. Outstanding customer service and what was more impressive was the fact we never actually had to request any of this, it was simply offered to us. If you want to feel welcome in a hotel this is the place to come! Another thing I found quite nice was a knock on the door each night with a card detailing the weather for the next day and also some free chocolate!LocationWe arrived at Union Station by Amtrak rail and the cab was 25 bucks to the hotel. About 8 miles I believe. Not too bad! The good thing is that this hotel is just round the corner from the main walk of fame strip in Hollywood. It was very convenient to go back and forth from the hotel to the local attractions on offer at Hollywood Blvd. Perfect location for what we wanted.OverallThis has to be the best overall hotel experience of my life. Whilst not necessarily being the best hotel in the world, The Magic Castle compensates by offering exceptional service and value for money, whilst also providing a location 2 minutes from the main features Hollywood has to offer. I would recommend this to anyone visiting Hollywood and I most certainly will return here if I am ever in the area. An absolute pleasure from start to finish.

<Author>brettystar
<Content>Depends what you are looking for My recent (and only) stay at The Magic Castle Hotel was mixed.The best asset that this hotel has is the staff - they truly are the most accommodating group of hotel staff that I have ever come across.I received the warmest, friendliest check in that I have ever had in my life. To me, the little touches is what differentiates good service from exceptional. To the welcome glass of lemonade, to the unlimited complimentary mini bar and the attitude that nothing you asked was any trouble - the service was first class. They make you feel like they are truly glad that you are their guest. I can only imagine that the owners must treat their staff well for all of them to be so happy.The worst asset of this hotel is the hotel itself. When I entered my room there was a very unusual and unpleasant odor in my room. I was only there for one night and was going to see 'Wicked' that evening so I didn't bother about asking to move rooms. However I got the feeling that the same smell would possibly be in the next room anyway. It was a mix of mustiness and cleaning product. It didn't go and was still there the next morning.The hotel room was extremely generous in size, especially for one person, however it was in bad shape. The kitchen and bathroom felt dirty; they weren't but they seemed like they were because they are so old.The security did not feel that great. From what I could see (and I could be wrong) there was only one door separating the guest rooms from the reception area (which anyone can walk into). I walked straight into the reception area and to my hotel room without anyone seeing me and as all the rooms have an outside entrance it kind of felt a little unsafe to me.It is close to Hollywood Boulevard however for those people visiting LA for the first time, I think it is better to stay in an area like West Hollywood or Beverly Hills.I spent one night at Magic Castle and another two at the Chamberlain in West Hollywood (I had always planned it this way), I felt so relieved when I got to the Chamberlain - I could just relax and not feel so on edge.Very long story short - the Magic Castle is conveniently located, has wonderful accommodating staff and offers a very good rate. However, when I visit LA I go there to relax by the pool and chill out. I think you can do this much better and in much more style at the Chamberlain (which charges a higher rate however).

<Author>robbandy
<Content>Great place for families to stay while visiting Hollywood My family of four (2 adults, 2 teens) stayed at the Magic Castle for 2 nights, and had a great experience. We had a suite with a bedroom with queen size bed and a pull out couch in the living room. The quality of the pullout couch wasn't wonderful, but it was fine for a teenager.The kitchen facilities were adequate although we didn't make full use of them. We got some takeout from a good local convenience store on Hollywood Blvd., about 10 minutes walk away, with a nice variety of prepared asian  western foods, but the oven, microwave, etc. in the kitchen were very handy. The room wasn't as modern as some generic hotel rooms, but it had a 40's/50's charm that you can't get in a modern hotel room, and certainly the rooms and bathrooms were clean.The staff was wonderful, even offered to drive us to the top of the hill to the Japanese restaurant, for us to admire the amazing view of Hollywood and L.A. We walked back down again, but I'm sure they would have picked us up had we requested it. Snacks were free upon request, as were DVD's from their extensive video library. The staff was always cheerful and friendly, and seem to enjoy working there!The location is great, about 2 blocks from the Chinese theater and Hollywood Blvd., but far enough away that noise was not really an issue, despite the hotel's location on a fairly busy street (although not a major boulevard). We didn't use the pool, but we did see a number of families using it. The nice breakfast buffet (included in the price) was a real plus; guests can either take their trays and sit by the pool, or bring them to their rooms to eat there. If you're looking for a luxurious Hollywood hotel stay (probably for a lot more money), don't stay here - but for budget-conscious travellers, especially families, looking for a good location and friendly atmosphere, this is a great place!

<Author>Theberd
<Content>Don't let the customer service at check-in fool you! When we arrived, I thought this was going to be a great place to stay. The staff was welcoming, and the hotel had lots of perks included. They gave us a welcome glass of lemonade and a list of DVDs you can borrow for free. The staff really went out of their way to provide excellent customer service. At least, that's how it seemed. THEN...We borrowed a DVD from the front desk. We went into the room and saw that the DVD player was missing. We went ahead and asked the girl at the front desk about it. She seemed very surprised and said there would be one in the room when we got back that evening. We got back to our room at about 10 pm, ready to settle into our movie. We were stopped by the guy at the front desk and told that they couldn't get the color to work on the DVD player, so we'd have to watch it in black and white. (Seriously?) This is when we realized that the customer service during our arrival was just an act. We thought, ok, that's ridiculous, but we'll suck it up and watch black and white. We turn on the system and realize the DVD player not only has no color but no sound. Additionally, the picture looked so pixelated, it was basically unwatchable. I called the front desk to ask how they could resolve this situation. The girl told me she'd have to call me back in 5 minutes so she could talk to the manager. Fine. 10 minutes later, she called to tell me that the room description did not guarantee a DVD player, so we were out of luck. Now I started getting upset. Most hotels would offer to move you to a different room or comp you in some way. NOT THE MAGIC CASTLE. I asked to be moved. She said she couldn't do that, so I asked to speak to the manager. Coincidentally, she had left 5 minutes before. She would talk to the supervisor, who was on his break. He'd call back in 5 minutes. 15 minutes later, she called back to say that the only room they had was a suite. If we wanted to move, we'd have to pay an extra $30 for the upgrade. Now I was getting really upset at the horrible service. I asked her if she would rather have an empty room and an upset customer. There's nothing I can do unless you want to pay the extra money. I told her there was no way I was paying extra to get the services that they had promised me when I checked in. 20 minutes go by, and she calls back to offer a complimentary move to the suite. It is now 11 pm! When we checked out, the girl at the front desk asked how our stay was. I told her we had some problems. Her response: I'm sorry to hear that. Seriously, that was it! No follow-up. No offers to make things right. Nothing. And the last straw was that when we got our bill, there was a $10 parking charge that is neither listed on their website nor mentioned when they give you the parking permit. Lastly, these rooms are renovated in the cheapest way I have ever seen. Door jams look like they've been broken into. The tubs were resurfaced and are now peeling. Etc, etc, etc.If you are going to stay here, HOPE against HOPE that you have no problems. They will *not* be solved here.

I cannot think of anything I would've changed about our stay at the Magic Castle Hotel. If we thought of it, they provided it, with a smile on their face.

<Author>M18elle
<Content>Almost Perfect!! My husband and I stayed at the Magic Castle hotel for 4 days and found the hotel staff were beyond helpful and friendly in fact they were amazing. Upon our arrival we were upgraded to a suite which was a pleasant surprise. We were at the back of the property on the top floor, overlooking the pool. We didn't use the pool but some kids used it whilst we were there and seemed to be having a ball. Now for the not so great:-We (or I should say my husband) had to struggle up the stairs with our cases without any assistanceThe bath had a little bit of mould around the grouting but the bathroom itself was otherwise clean they alos provided fluffy robesThe furniture was a little scruffy in places and could do with being updated. This was true of the hotel in general, it is in need of an upgrade especially the main reception, walkways and stairs. All in all these things were not a big deal and really didn't spoil our stay. The suite we stayed in had a fully equiped kitchen: microwave cooker, fridge freezer with ice tray coffee maker. The living area was spacious with generous seating a tv and satelite and DVD player. The bedroom was very comfortable with a king size bed lovely! it also had ample wardrobe space and tv and satelite and lovely lighting. We could not hear much road noise as we were at the back but I have to say that the walls are very thin and could almost make out the conversation the people below us were having. But that said, luckily we did not have any noisy neighbours during our stay. The hotel is in a great location within walking distance to the Kodak Theatre and other attractions, most tours pick up from this hotel too. Most attractions were no more than 20 mins drive away.I think it's fair to say that what made the stay good for us was the amazing staff (we have stayed at some top hotels but I have to say that the staff here rival those) who were more that happy to help with anything from turning on the heating system almost immediately when asked and booking our tour which was brill!!. Oh and not to forget the free mini bar snacks and drinks that were availiable 24hrs and DVD supplies.If it's luxury you're after then this is not the place for you. But if you want to be treated like royalty be comfortable in knowing that the Magic Castle is not only value for money but is a great place to stay for seeing Los Angeles, Beverley Hill and such places.

<Author>Andrewuk56
<Content>Excellent service and great location We stayed for 16 nights and found the location to be excellent for all the tourist sites, especially in the Hollywood / Beverly Hills area, being only a short walk from the chinese theatre and Kodak theatre on Hollywood BoulevardWe were very impressed with the staff who were friendly and very helpful , the service from the staff was without fault, the best we have experienced in a long time.The pool was clean and well maintained and heated, very nice indeed. The Magic Castle Club adjoining the hotel gives membership to hotel guests but bear in mind if you have children you will only be allowed to take them in for Sunday Brunch, all other times is Adult only. Having said that the Brunch was excellent and great magic shows to accompany it. There is a strict dress code but relaxed a little for the Brunch.So why only the average rating ?Safe parking in underground car park but $10 per day and we were charged for all 16 nights although we only parked in the garage on 13 of the 16 days being away in San Diego and Las Vegas for a few days.Our big dissapointment was our room, room 108 which was a suite but in a bad position being on the gorund floor the view from the windows was a derelict falling down fence at the back of the hotel. The suite was also in bad need of decoration and refurbishment, no handles on the wardrobe doors, loose electrical sockets, the fridge wasn't working although was quickly replaced. The bathroom was the worst being in a very poor state of repair, although clean. The Plumbing system was very noisy so if anyone in an adjoining room decide to have a shower in the early hours you could not fail to wake up.We didn't see inside any other rooms, but would recommend you ask for a pool view room.There is no bar or restaurant, except in the adjoining club but an adequate continental style breakfast is servved in the lobby, you can sit around the pool or take it to your room, although we found it hard to get a table by the pool as there were only a small number and in great demand.I would certainly recommend this hotel on the grounds of service and location alone, but bear in mind your room may be quite the same as the photos on the website !Andrew ParkerSuffolkEnglandUK

<Author>PATwinMom
<Content>Good deal for families! This hotel is a former apt bldg which provides clean but somewhat shabby rooms. We were traveling with teenagers and needed more than one sleeper sofa for them, but were not eager to spring for 2 hotel rooms, so having both an extra bedroom and a sleeper sofa in the living room was ideal. We reserved a 2-bedroom unit, which is recommended if you are troubled by noise, as these units are in the back (away from the street). We also appreciated the heated swimming pool, the free breakfast (fruit, scones, muffins, juices, coffee), the laundry facilities, the free water bottles and snacks and the cheerful hospitality of the staff (who readily offered advice, printed directions to sites and help with dinner reservations). It was also convenient having a reasonably priced parking facility ($10 a night) underneath the hotel. (L.A. is huge and sprawling, so you need a car to see anything beyond the immediate Hollywood area.) I would choose something newer and nicer if it were just the two of us, but if you are traveling with kids who are too big to share a sleeper sofa (and the local suite hotels I tried informed me that they did not have additional cots at their L.A. locations), this works out well.

<Author>Ruch08
<Content>Great location and excellent staff Located a couple of blocks off the Walk of Fame, this is a wonderful place to stay in... We stayed in a 2-BR suite, which was very spacious and simply decorated. Their staff is very pleasent and helpful. The front desk did some research for us and guided us around the place.. They also serve a breakfast (included in the room fare) - it's not much, juices, muffins and the like but enough to start your morning - although this is served out in the reception area; you can serve yourself and take it into the room or eat by the pool..There were a few drawbacks, like most hotels in L.A. the building is old and the bathrooms could use an upgrade (not too shabby though). Our room was bang on the street, which meant a lot of noise from the constant traffic all through the night - so if you're a light sleeper beware. But the spacious rooms, the attentive staff, and the location are a must-do. And, one can see the Hollywood sign from the back of the building.

<Author>former_LA_resident
<Content>Nice perks but needs touching up We stayed at the MC Hotel primarily to take advantage of the opportunity to visit the Magic Castle (private club next door). The location is excellent for a Hollywood destination, indeed. And the Magic Castle club experience was one-of-a-kind. I was curious to see how nice the hotel would be due to its #1 ranking on this site. In this case, it seems to be a victim of overinflated expectations. Yes, there are nice perks and the staff is wonderfully attentive, friendly and helpful. As we had to leave early to catch a flight, they even had some pastries bagged for us (I had asked them prior to our visit). However, the physical hotel is dated and needs some attention to detail and updating. Caulking in bathrooms, molding, patio surrounding pool all need some work. Also we could clearly hear our neighbors through the suite door connecting the 2 rooms. One last important note....there is no elevator to the second floor rooms and the layout is awkward. This would be particularly difficult for someone a bit older carrying a suitcase.All in all, the room was very comfortable and we enjoyed the flat-screen television. Pretty fair overall, but beware of some shortcomings and you'll be fine.

<Author>789123
<Content>Hmm wonder what you are thinking We just came back from our stay in Hollywood California, 2 days ago and our last night was in the Magic Castle. Everything people say about their staff is true. Wonderful people very very accommodating. The place was clean but needed lots and lots of work. Its really too bad the owners don't upgrade their property to match the high standard of their staff. It is really old style plaster rooms with old plywood cupboards in the kitchen and hallway, this is not retro just old. An old apartment turned into a hotel room with very little character in the rooms. We had a room with 1 bedroom and kitchen. didn't sleep at all as there was a road right outside the bedroom window which was busy enough to keep us awake most of the night. The TV in the bedroom needs to be raised so you can see it while lying in bed. The bathroom had lino with burnt cigarette marks, the mirror had black marks on the mirror...like when it is old., the shower curtain didn't cover the entire tub area so as you shower you need to keep moving it around. The lighting in the suite needs to be improved it was quite dim at night. We could hear the people in the room next to us, very clearly and embarassingly I might add. As you can see in the pictures there are no draperies on the windows thus the sound does bounce around. I would recommend it if you need to stay in downtown hollywood this may be your cleanest and safest choice. as it is right next to the main attractions, the Kodak theater and such... but bring your earplugs.

<Author>wishiwasretired
<Content>great getaway in hollywood We spent three nights at the Magic Castle Hotel in January, enjoying the hotel and the Magic Castle itself. Our room was large, very minimalist, very accomodating. Comfortable beds with wonderful cotton sheets and great pillows. Really special products in the bathroom. We had a full kitchen, nicely equipped including a full size refrigerator. Our room was a junior suite, and it's the only one we don't recommend for anyone who likes quiet - it is located above the lobby which has automatic sliding doors that open at the slightest movement near them. A nice continental breakfast is served in the lobby every morning, and as people took their food we heard the door constantly. It was the last room available when I made the reservation. All the rooms open on a courtyard, with a pool in the middle surrounded by lounge chairs and tables for eating. Lovely!Hotel is on Franklin Avenue - perfect location for walking everywhere in Hollywood. This was the first time we visited LA and didn't have to rent a car. Staying at the hotel gives you access for eight people to the Magic Castle, a private club featuring magicians doing shows in small theaters, tiny elegant rooms, and close up at tables scattered throughout the club. We also enjoyed dinner at Yamashiro, Cal-Asian cuisine, located up the hill with an incredible view of LA and delicious food. The hotel shuttle took us to both places. For free. The manager sent us a complimentary appetizer. We felt so welcome, so cared for.Incredible value, reasonable price, and the best staff we've ever seen. They were as attentive, pleasant and efficient as at hotels like The Ritz and Four Seasons. There are no elevators, only two floors, and the staff took care of all six bags with no problem. The one error made was fixed with sincere apologies and the hotel paid for our cab to the airport. Overall, not a fancy hotel, but so comfortable and enjoyable it now ranks as one of our favorites anywhere! It feels like you live there, in a nice apartment, and have the help and attention of a staff who can advise you on local restaurants, answer all your questions, even find you a snack in the middle of the night - complimentary of course!We've been visiting LA since our daughter moved there in '03 - every visit will now include a stay at the Magic Castle Hotel.

<Author>jonphil
<Content>Home Away From Home This is my home away from home and everytime I'm in L.A., with or without my family, I stay here. Sure, sometimes the bathtub is a little rusted and the shelf in the bathroom falls down and the lights from cars going up to the Japanese restaurant on the hill in back of the hotel shine in, but this place has character! As one who appreciates Hollywood history and a place to just crash after a crazy day in L.A., this place is perfect. The staff is incredibly nice and helpful and the little amenities - the cold drink when you check in, the cider at night, the music playing when you go into the room - are great. The place reeks of Hollywood History and it is a great jumping off spot for Hollywood and the Valley (don't try to get on the 101 at rush hour from the hotel!). Franklin Avenue itself is historic - parts of Rebel Without A Cause was filmed here, Janis Joplin died next door, Yamashiro, the Japanese Restaurant on the hill has an incredible history, and Ozzie and Harriet's (and Ricky's) house where they lived during their long-running popular TV show is just a few blocks away on Franklin. The parking is a little tough, but what really makes this place so special is its location to the Hollywood tourist stuff, it's access to the Magic Castle (no jeans!), and most of all, its staff. It ain't first class luxury, but it's homey, clean and incredibly comfortable and roomy .

<Author>Julesbusiness
<Content>Superb in every aspect The Magic Castle far exceeded any expectations that I had when I booked. Upon arrival there were two members of staff on reception who genuinely took an interest in me, where I was from, how was the journey, what did I want to see/do in LA etc. As it was a hot day, they immediately gave me a complimentary drink and provided me with lots of advice about how to get around the area (as I didn鈥檛 have a hire car) as well as bus timetables and maps.Following this, I was shown to my room and was amazed at the size of it. It was as big as an apartment that you would be quite happy to live in. There was an open plan living room complete with TV, radio, sofa, comfy stools that lead into a dining area with full sized dining table and then on to a kitchen complete with sink, cupboards, microwave, full size fridge and a fresh coffee maker. In the back was the bedroom with two full size built in wardrobes and large comfortable bed and in the next room the bath/shower.My room was on the ground floor near reception so the view looked out onto the pool that is in the centre of the complex. A continental breakfast was available in the reception area and you could eat it in the sunshine at the tables around the pool. An internet service is also available in this area.The hotel is in an excellent location, just five minutes walk to the Chinese Theatre and all of the other attractions of Hollywood Boulevard. As mentioned, I didn鈥檛 have a car, but getting around was not a problem using the Magic Castle as a base as it is only about 7 minutes walk to Hollywood/Highland metro station, 4 minutes walk to a bus stop on Hollywood Boulevard that has buses that go to numerous places such as Sunset Strip etc and close to a number of attractions such as the Kodak Theatre and a stunning view of the Hollywood sign.When it was time to check out, the receptionist was genuinely interested in how I enjoyed my stay, what I thought of the accommodation, where I was heading to next and if I knew how to get to get transport to my next destination. When I told her I would be taking an internal flight, she said, 鈥渟ounds like you are in for a long day鈥?and gave me a large bag of snacks and drinks free of charge. Perfect. It was then just a 7 minute walk to the metro station that took me directly to LAX and onwards.Overall, this is an excellent hotel in a great location with superb staff, incredible rooms and provides an experience that exceeds expectations.

<Author>WorldTripster
<Content>Sad for rest of LA hotels that this is #1 We stayed for four nights over Christmas. There were some really great things about the hotel - staff seemed very jolly, the free mini bar; basically you can select soft drinks, chips, candies from a huge selection - for free, 24 hours a day. The continental breakfast wasn't really gourmet, but certainly there were some nice pastries and hey - it's free! On the downside our room was barely big enough for cat swinging and the recent renovations themselves look like they need some renovating. Our main complaint was that our room was really noisy. The walls are paper thin and, apparently unlike the other guests, we are in the minority as we like to sleep until 9.30am or so when we are on vacation. Sadly we were woken daily at 7am by stomping up and down stairs outside, doors slamming and whoever happened to be in the room next door - thanks to an adjoining door they literally sounded as though they were in the same room as us. Also slightly off-putting - the ashtray for our floor was right outside our window and by our air conditioning unit so a few times we had the A/C on only to find moments later our room smelling of smoke. Also pretty annoying was the lack of regulation of hot water in the shower - every day there was leaping in and out of the stream of water from either being scalded or frozen. It's a sad indictment of LA hotels that this is ranked the best hotel - it is not the worst I have ever stayed in, but it's no star. All in all the location is pretty good, and rates reasonable, if you are a smoker that doesn't need much sleep/privacy and is OK with an invigorating game of hot/cold in the shower every morning this is the perfect place for you!

<Author>Samianos
<Content>The friendly staff make for a great stay This hotel is a bargain. Great location in Hollywood, 5 mins walk to Grauman's Chinese Theatre, underground car park (you need a car in LA), big rooms to suit a family with a couple of kids. This used to be a small apartment block, so the rooms have separate bedrooms, walk-in wardrobes, large sitting rooms with sofa bed (for the kids) and fully equipped kitchen areas. Excellent continental breakfast is served by the pool and there is a free mini-bar (yes you did read this right). Basically you can get whatever non-alcoholic drink and snacks you want from the reception for no charge. But the best feature are the staff, They will bend over backwards to serve and nothing is too much trouble for them. After they make sure you have directions and maps for your destination, they practically force in to your hands cold bottles of water to take with you. The building is in need of moderate maintenance, and I could possibly knock a star off for that reason But the beds are really comfortable, and as i said the staff really make this place. Definitely going back!

<Author>SnoopyTennessee
<Content>Friendly Hotel in a Great Location We recently stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel. The hotel is located in Hollywood, a couple of blocks from the Highland Mall and Grauman's Chinese Theater. It isn't fancy, but that is part of it's charm. It gives you the feel as if you are living in L.A. The staff is very friendly. Where most hotels charge you an outrageous price for water, sodas and snacks, they give them to you. Whenever you want something to drink or a snack, all you have to do is ask at the front desk. The pool is heated. A swim at night is a great way to relax. The breakfast was good. They have cereal, yogurt and fresh pastries. The scones were really good. If you get a chance, make a dinner reservation at the Magic Castle. You normally have to be a member or be invited to visit it. Hotel guests are allowed to visit it as long as you eat dinner there. It was a lot of fun.When we are in the L.A. area, we will be sure to stay at the Magic Castle Hotel.

<Author>klingoneddie
<Content>Cant beat the staff here Stayed here for three nights in Sept as part of our tour of southern Califonia. I have to say that the location of the hotel really was excellent, only 3/4 minutes walk from Manns Chinese Theatre and 4/5 mins to the Metro (very handy for getting to /from Universal Studios). Hotel parking was an underground secure park for only $9 a day. Thats a bargain in this part of town, believe me. Found the hotel really easily from the Freeway, just ensure you have printed off a map from Expedia or bought a street map beforehand.Arrival and checkin was quick and made more pleasurable with the refreshments made available by the reception staff.Staff--let me tell you about the staff.You will find it very hard to find a hotel in which all the staff are so helpful, cheerful and welcoming. Sean and Megan deserve a special mention here, in particular Sean who really went the extra mile. (on checkout, Sean made up a bag of goodies for us for our drive to Vegas)Every evening one of the staff would come to your room to check everything was OK and distribute chocolates!!Every question posed to the staff (you know , those boring ones about where to go, how to get there etc, the ones they had heard a thousand times before) were met with a cheerful smile and enthusistic reply. I was so impressed with the service I had to tell Gretchen, the desk manager ,how godd her people were.Complimentary breakfast was good and set you up nicely for the day.Pool was small but cool, just what you need in LA.Only downside to this place is that it does need some refurbishment BUT rooms are clean and comfortable. (this is the reason I have given 4 stars rather than 5) The bed was great .Great views from the restaurant at the top of the hill. Shuttle bus will take you up there.We went as a family of four, kids both over 20 but we all enjoyed the stay.I would happily stay here again and recommend to others.

<Content>Alternative but we loved it!! I chose the hotel becuse my older daughter who lives in LA wanted to go to The Magic Castle and based on reviews here and elsewhere. It's definitely alternative but we loved it. My husband goes for luxury business class hotels and that it isn't. My kids were delighted with free and bountiful DVD selection and mini-bar (cokes, snacks, etc.). Bottled water, too, was free on request. The service is, shall I use the word?....yes...awesome!!! My husband bragged about the hotel to his friends. And, of course, you can visit the Magic Castle next door (also wonderful brunch and show)and the incredible Japanese restaurant on the hill above. If you stay here, do all three as they are part of the same property and should'nt be missed. A fantastic experience.

<Author>rjscCaymanIslands
<Content>The best hotel staff we've ever experienced What a magical place this hotel is. It's not fancy or luxurious, but it's clean, bright, the rooms are large, and the staff is absolutely wonderful. The hotel has a family feel to it, although there were singles there as well. The pool was great, right in the middle of the courtyard. And, late in the afternoon, a staff member comes and offers lemonade and popsicles to the people in and around the pool - free of charge! Upon arrival to Magic Castle, the reception staff offer champagne flutes with lemonade in them. Breakfast is complimentary and quite adequate - cereals, fruit, pastries, bread, spreads, coffee, juice, etc. Soft drinks and snacks are available at the front desk, any time of day, and are also complimentary!We could walk to Hollywood Blvd. in 5 minutes, where we visited Graumann's Theater, the Walk of Fame, the Kodak Theater and lots of interesting shops. There is also a Metro stop right there, so you can take the subway wherever you need to go.What made the Magic Castle Hotel so special to us was the staff. On our second last day, we found out that our pet cat (we've had her 12 years) was very ill and would probably pass away at any moment. I informed the front desk staff that we would have to check out a day early and they were very understanding. A few minutes after I had gone back to my room, one of the staff knocked on the door and gave us a little card they had made for us, saying they hoped our cat would be alright. They also gave us a little stuffed mouse for her to play with.So to Gretchen, Adam, Shawn and (I think) Daphne, thank you so much for your kindness and hospitality. We will definitely return!!And to anyone considering staying at the Magic Castle, go for it.We've never experienced such helpful and friendly people as we did there.(PS: Our cat is still hanging in, but she doesn't have much time left. But she was so happy to see us.)

<Author>99bottles
<Content>Out of Date - Appeared Dirty - Warning - I'm about to pan this place. I know people don't like it when people give bad reviews. If you read my review you will probably think well that guy is picky or a snob or this guy is an idiot that has never travelled because look at all the positive reviews.Just so you know where I am coming from and can better judge whether or not you believe my bad review. I'm a 30 year old professional and have done a lot of travelling - some for business and a lot for fun. I'm from Toronto. I've travelled extensively in the United States. I know that this place is a 3 star hotel and not a 5 star hotel. I understand that in a major North American city that $180 is not a lot to spend for a nights stay in a downtown location. All I expect from a 3 star hotel is: clean and current decor in the lobby and rooms but nothing flashy, basic amenities like internet and a desk to do some work on, and reasonable staff that are polite and moderately helpful. If this place had all of these things I would have given it a 5 rating or said it was excellent.I was on my honeymoon and I would not come back to this hotel. My main complaint is the rooms. I'd rather just spend an extra $75 or $100 a night to stay somewhere decent. If I had known what this hotel was really like I would have gladly dropped the extra cash somewhere else.I paid about $180 bucks for a Thursday night stay - too expensive for what it was.- Cons -The pictures on the website are misleading because they don't show you the grungy bathrooms, noisy window unit air-conditioners, or stained carpets. The room also had a musty smell which I might expect in Mexico or South America but not in the United States.I was pretty disgusted with our first room and asked to be moved. The next room was still grungy but slightly better. Honestly, this place needs to change the carpets in the rooms. It could use a complete overhaul, however, it definitely needs new carpets. I know that the rooms are probably just as clean or dirty as any other hotel but when the carpets are beat up and stained it just makes you feel like you need to wear shoes in the room at all times. Both the rooms had a dirty $30 a night motel feel about them.- Pros - Good location to do all the tacky Hollywood stuff (visit Mann's theatre, the walk of fame, etc.). Friendly and helpful staff during the day time. The night time staff llooked like they were into goth, demons and depression. Maybe I'm getting old but I'm not into hotel staff having lip rings and blue hair (I don't know if they were friendly or helpful because I didn't bother talking to them). The pool was open 24 hours (but looked pretty nasty and was more of kids urinal than a pool). Free WiFi for your laptop. Nice soaps, creams, and stuff. Pretty comfortable bed and bedding. Free snacks and DVDs that are available in the lobby. - How is this #2 on TripAdvisor???? -Because of this hotel and it's #2 rating in Los Angeles, I don't know whether I will ever trust TripAdvisor ratings again. Are travellers so enamoured by friendly staff and free candy bars that they overlook the rooms being disgusting and in drastic need of renovation. The only thing magical about this place is that it somehow got a #2 rating on TripAdvisor.Don't stay here if you want to spend anytime at all in your room or at the hotel. This place is NOT romantic. It might be okay for famillies with kids because you can get rooms with kitchenettes to save on dining costs. We just had a room without the kitchen.Overall my 2 rating is generous.

<Author>daisygirl59
<Content>Offbeat but fun and comfortable Overall our experience at the Magic Castle Hotel was very good, and my two kids both said they wanted to come back - and I did not hear that comment about either of the other two hotels where we stayed in LA. This is a hotel with history and personality. It's not another Holiday Inn Express or whatever. It is also in the city, folks - yes, you will see homeless people, and yes, you will see interesting street life on Hollywood Boulevard. If that scares or upsets you, I would advise picking another area in which to sightsee. Hollywood may be undergoing some gentrification but it is not Disneyland. As everyone says, the front desk staff members go out of their way to make sure you are satisfied. I saw the manager all over the place all the time, not hiding back in an office. We had a king bed suite and the space was just huge. The kitchen and bathroom were very clean; I had no problem at all there. My favorite spot was the balcony over the pool, where you could sit and read the newspaper, watch the kids in the pool, or just drink your morning coffee before another day of sightseeing. Breakfast included the yummiest scones ever and top-notch coffee. Now, on the other hand, it is a remodeled older former apartment building and there are some irritants. The stairs and railings need paint, and some coverings on the stairs are coming loose. The carpet in the hallways is getting worn. There was a crack in the paint on one wall in our kitchen, and a small hole in a window. The stopper in the bathroom sink didn't work. Some of the housekeeping was a little spacey - plenty of forks and knives in the utensil drawer but no spoons, no glasses replaced one day, no bath mat another day. But if it really deeply mattered to me I am sure the desk would have sent up more spoons or another bath mat immediately. I think this is a great little hotel, and I'll be sad if it gets sold and turned into yet another condo development or generic hotel. The best option would be new owners who could spruce it up without raising the prices too much or losing the great staff members. Thanks again for a nice stay.

<Author>Ward44
<Content>Home away from home. My Husband and I have just returned from a two week stay at the Magic Castle Hotel in Los Angeles. We need to say that this is one of the BEST Hotels that we have ever stayed in ( in LA or in other countries). When we arrived we received a glass of ice cold lemonade, which was so welcome after a long journey. The exeptional friendliness of the staff creates a warm and personal experience. You actually feel like old friends!!!!All of the staff went out of their way to make any requests that we had, happen. The front desk staff (Big hugs to Daphne, Christen, Shawn and Adam), arranged restaurant bookings for us as well as ordering cabs. We celebrated our Birthdays while staying at the hotel and we recieved a bottle of wine and some goodies. A very nice personal touch!!Our room was clean, comfortable and the bed was so lovely. It seemed huge!!! Fresh towels were provided everyday, if we so wished, and the shower was so powerful that it certainly woke us up in a morning. There is a complimentary breakfast every morning in the courtyard. The scones are wonderful and the coffee was always hot, fresh and abundent. The pool is attractive, clean and heated. Towels are provided by the hotel and there are pool toys available for the kids. Snacks and soft drinks are complimentary from the reception at any time of the day ( we have never known a Hotel do this), which is so nice if you want to lounge by the pool, watch a film in your room or you are just feeling a bit peckish. We will certainly be returning to the hotel. It has so many assets. Not only is it friendly it is close to all amenities and feels safe and secure. Tip...you have got to go to the Yamashiro restaurant. It provides some of the best views in LA... and the food and the staff are great. The Hotel provides a complimentary shuttle service to the restaurant and as a guest of the Hotel they will arrange the booking for you. Another nice touch!. We had a perfect 2 week stay and have recommended the Magic Castle Hotel to our family and friends. Thanks for making our holiday special!!

<Author>Love_2_Travel233
<Content>Staff went above and beyond the call of duty! Date: August 6, 2007Reviewer: Kitchener, OntarioMy son and I stayed at the Magic Castle hotel from July 20 to 24. This hotel was on a list recommended by the school that my son was attending an open house for as it was only a 15 minute walk from the school. I thought the hotel would be bigger and was a little disappointed when we arrived. It reminded me of the show Melrose Place with the rooms all surrounding the pool. But the staff put us at ease the minute we arrived and the good thing about a smaller hotel is that the staff get to recoginize you very quickly and they also know who doesn't belong there. They were so friendly and greeted every time we walked by.My son and I had a one bedroom suite with dining area and kitchen and 2 queen beds that were very comfortable.The rooms were very clean and large. The shower was amazing as it had so much pressure that washing my hair was so easy. 45 minutes before we were checking out and our limo ( that the hotel had arranged for us) was to pick us up, I dropped a glass in the sink and it broke and I sliced my finger quite badly and I could not get the bleeding to stop. My son went down to the front desk and staff came to my aid and said I needed stitches and they would drive me to a local clinic. Panic set in as I was afraid we would miss our flight. The hotel manager drove me and my son to a clinic she goes to and that was 5 minutes from the hotel and when we arrived she explained my delimma. They saw me immediately and she waited in the waiting room for me and helped my son with all the paper work. 30 minutes later with 5 stitches in my finger we were on our way back to the hotel, were the limo driver had been contacted and asked to wait for us. He did and we were only 15 minutes off schedule and we made our flight with time to spare. I can't thank the management and hotel staff enough for taking care of me and keeping my son calm through this unusual event. I would recommend this hotel even if I didn't injure my finger and we will definately be staying there again when my son is attending school there.

<Author>JamaicaPhil
<Content>Unmatched Customer Service...Excellent! The Magic Castle is a quaint, small hotel (42 rooms I think) just steps off the Hollywood strip and within very short walking distance to the Chinese theater, Kodak theater, etc. Our family of 4 (kids: 15 and 11) stayed 4 nts in late July in a spacious 1-bedroom suite...more like a 1-bedroom apartment. Beds were cozy, climate control and wireless network (free) were reliable and cleanliness, impeccable. This is an older building and nothing fancy but nevertheless, clean, tastefully decorated and spacious.As you have read from previous reviews, the most redeeming quality of this hotel is its Customer Service. Sort of a throwback, of sorts, to the hotels of old where customers were treated as royalty and where the entire staff are all on the same page when it comes to taking personal responsibilty for exceeding customer expectations. Very rarely do you find this prevailing attitude among staff in American hotels. The hotel offers free beverages, movies and snacks unlike most hotels that nickel and dime its customers to squeeze out every bit of profit imaginable. Here, they truley understand that their customers are their best advertisers.Needless to say, we had a great time at the Magic Castle and overall we had a blast in Hollywood. Special thanks to Daphne Springs who went above and beyond to help make this a vacation we will never forget. We were sad to leave this place but look forward to returning.

We stayed at the Roosevelt the last time we visited L.A and although it was nice, Magic Castle is the better option.

<Author>snazzyjan
<Content>Awesome Customer Service! I was thoroughly impressed with the amount of service this hotel gives their customers! All the staff is friendly and accomodating. As soon as you enter they give you a fruity drink (non alcoholic) and welcome you to the hotel. Around 5pm every day, a staff member comes around and gives mints and a card with tomorrow's weather on it. At their 7-10am complimentary breakfast (with real food from a local bakery (pastries, toast, cereal, coffee, tea), not all that greasy stuff you get at other hotels) the manager always walks around and asks how you're doing and how they can help you. The concierge desk is very helpful with anything from directions, to food, to drinks, to Free DVD rentals! They have a heated pool in the center that's 24hrs. The setup of the building is very community oriented. The room itself - is hooked up! When you walk in they have soft music playing on the stereo in the living room. Yes a living room! You don't just have a bedroom, but a kitchen, living area with a pullout couch, a spacious bathroom, tons of closet space... it's like an apartment more than a hotel room. They really go out of their way to make you feel at home. The location is perfect - you're a block or so away from Grauman's Chinese Theater, the Kodak Theatre and all these shops and food places. There's some museums in the area. If you're not from the area - bring with you a detailed street map. It's really easy to get lost around there, and the traffic is ridiculous - but you'll have a great time! Also - if you want to get into the Magic Castle Club - make sure you have the right dress code! Dresses for ladies, Blazer and tie for gentlemen.... When I come back to LA, if I need to find a place to stay - I'm definitely booking a room here again! :)

<Author>mini
<Content>Enjoyable Stay - Service Nice; Comfy Stay The Magic Castle is at a good location in Hollywood - walkable distance to Hollywood and Highland; Mann's Chinese Theater, and other points of interest in the area. It is next to the Magic Castle - which is where you can have a nice dinner (or more casual Sunday brunch) and watch some magic shows.The rooms are large - ours had a kitchen, living room, bathroom, and bedroom. The rooms are comfortable - however at some point will need to be updated. Beds were comfortable and we enjoyed our stay. Swimming pool is open 24 hours and the included continental breakfast in the morning is a nice touch.The juice drink on check out was a very nice tough. The hotel also prides itself on service! We were there on my birthday. It was so nice to find a birthday card in the room from the hotel...and a wonderful small cake in the refrigerator. They also let the Magic Castle know that it was my birthday and they made me feel special for Sunday brunch! Overall, service is quite nice; and it is very personalized touch. Enjoyable.One major note about the hotel - you need to be comfortable climbing stairs for almost all the rooms. We were on the 2nd floor and soon got used to climbing the 3 sets of stairs to reach our room. The rooms are large for families....and nice for young families...some have balconies....however do take note about the stairs.In general, the hotel knows where it needs to please its customers. It also seems to know its downsides and compensates by very personal and nice service. Its not the best in the area - but is a comfortable - and enjoyable stay.

<Content>June 28, 2007 I have plenty of fabulous things to say about the Magic Castle Hotel in Hollywood. The moment we walked in we were greeted by Shawn at the Front Desk who was very friendly and helpful. We arrived a couple hours before the typical check-in and asked if our room was available (standard queen room) but it was not, so he provided a free upgrade to a one bedroom suite! The suite was very clean and spacious, they even turn down your bed at night and leave chocolates on the pillows with the weather forecast for the next day. Megan at the front desk was also quite helpful, booking reservations at a nearby restaurant, offering us a ride to the restaurant and sending us a free appetizer! The breakfast spread is better than the continental breakfasts most large chain hotels offer, and the croissants and scones were very tasty! Location is another key point, one block from Kodak Theatre, Graumanns, and shopping at the Hollywood/Highland Centre. I would not hesitate to recommend this hotel to anyone!

<Author>kmbmommy
<Content>Great location, excellent service The Magic Castle Hotel was all that it was built up to be on tripadvisor. Make a reservation here and enjoy your vacation.The location in Hollywood is terrific. You can walk to the Hollywood and Highland Center, the Chinese Theatre, the Kodak Theatre, Hollywood Walk of Fame, etc. For this part of town, their price is more affordable than most and you get your money's worth in space. We reserved a one-bedroom suite and it included a living room with a pull-out sofa, a dining area, a full kitchen, patio with table and chairs, small bathroom and a separate bedroom with a king bed. One sign of their excellent customer service was that they had already placed a rollaway in the living room for my son before we arrived. The room had almost more closet space than my own house! The morning breakfast was adequate with offerings of delicious scones and assorted pastries, yogurt, fresh fruit, cereal and milk, juices and coffee. Our children enjoyed the heated swimming pool in the courtyard.The room itself needed some updating. The telephones, furnishings (bed and dresser, sofa bed) and the bathroom were very outdated. The A/C in the bedroom also was not sufficient to cool the room. My in-laws had a studio room which was more updated than ours and they were quite pleased with my choice of hotels!We loved this hotel and would stay here in a heartbeat if ever in LA again. Why? Because of the wonderful staff and excellent customer service! The staff were ALL very customer-friendly. Service with a smile must be their motto. When we checked in late on a Thursday evening, they offered us an orange soda spritzer in champagne glasses to welcome us to the Magic Castle Hotel. They gave us a menu of snacks (incl. sodas, bottled water, candy, and chips) available free any time of day (we took full advantage of these throughout our stay). They offered us popsicles as we lounged by the pool. They lent us free DVD's for viewing. They also printed out information on a world premiere happening on Hollywood Boulevard. By far, the nicest touch was the birthday cake and balloons they had for my mother-in-law in her room when we checked in on her birthday. Their covered parking is very secure and we took advantage of the added bonus of entrance to the Magic Castle for Saturday brunch. That is a must do as well!!! Thank you, Magic Castle Hotel and Staff, for a wonderful stay!!!

Breakfasts were nice and fresh and the staff very helpful, but overall it did not meet our expectations.

<Author>pippippooray
<Content>An excellent base to discover LA - lovely hotel This turned out to be a great base for a weeks holiday in LA, a very good, family hotel in a fabulously convenient location and not too expensive (at least not when we were there). Very close to all the action in Hollywood. Carparking was not too expensive at 9 dollars a day - a lot of the other hotels in our price range that I looked at were much more per day. Breakfast buffet was nice (basically cereals, pastries, cakes) and available til 10am, after that staff would offer coffee, soft drinks etc which was very nice. The hotel staff were really friendly and helpful. The room was a good size (we just had a double room not one of the apartments). Access to the rooms is off various little stairways round a courtyard with a swimming pool, so going up and down various small flights of stairs was unavoidable. The walls were quite thin - you could hear a lot of what was going on outside and in next-door rooms, but it was generally pretty quiet when we were there and we werent bothered by it. The bed was really comfortable, the aircon unit pretty efficient, the bathroom clean and good sized, with a huge shower, plenty of nice fluffy towels. A complimentary local newspaper was left on our doorstep every morning which was nice. We were generally out sightseeing all day so it was absolutely fine as a base to come back to at night, crash out and set off refreshed in the morning. We were given excellent suggestions for local places to eat, there are loads of nearly restaurants, bars, diners, cafes. there's a pay as you go internet kiosk in the courtyard. The hotel doesnt appear to sell alcohol.The Magic Castle Club is apparently well worth a visit, but you'll need to take smart clothes (jacket and tie for men, cocktail dress or trouser suit for women is what they state the dress code to be) so we didnt actually go there. We would definitely stay at this hotel again - it isnt a luxury hotel, but it is clean, comfortable, family friendly, and well located, with the friendliest and most helpful staff.

<Author>jellyb
<Content>Good with Illusion of Something Better There are two ways one could write a review of the Magic Castle Hotel, from a perspective of comparison with other properties in the area and from a perspective of comparison with all hotels in general. This is the only property I've stayed at in the Hollywood area so I can't compare it to other nearby properties but feel that would be the fairest way to evaluate this property.I research my vacations to death and hadn't run across many properties that had such a uniform, overwhelming positive response so I felt this was a no-brainer. Three words best decribe this place: Location, Staff, and Location. Did I say location?As far as I can tell, if you want to be within walking distance of the center of the Hollywood Universe, this is a superb choice (although there is really not much to see besides the Walk of Fame, Chinese Theater, and the new Mall at Hollywood  Highland - otherwise this area is pretty cheesy/touristy definitely something you can see in a half day.) Nevertheless it is a good base from which to explore other surrounding areas.I'd say the reviews in general overhype this place a tad too much. The staff is on the ball and provide little 'extras' here and there like the champagne glass of lime pop when you check in, popsicles at the pool, the chocolates and weather report card in the evening. I guess these little things really impress people as many other properties don't make the small effort to do similar things. As a result, these little things they do help to give the illusion (yes pun intended) that this property is something very special. The reality is the rooms (at least ours and from reading some of the other reviews) are spacious and clean, but bit run-down and apparently have probably had only minor cosmetic rennovations in recent years such as a coat of paint and maybe some new carpet. Most (not all) of the furnishings are sparse, cheap, dated, and in some cases tired looking. There are many small aspects (although minor) of the room which were in disrepair such as peeling paint on the bathroom ceiling, linoleum coming up around the tub, slidding shudder off it's hinges (which maintenance didn't fix properly), etc. The bathroom is small, basic, and very dated with very old fixtures. It appears the only thing they've done recently to the bathroom is slap some cheap, ugly Corian on the countertop. Water pressure is good and hot water doesn't run out. A big plus.Bedroom bed was comfortable, although a little on the firm side, too firm for my wife. The mattress on the pull-out was a joke. No way anyone over 50 pounds could get a good night's rest on it. Definitely need a new pullout mattress.  The rooms have a very (I'm guessing) 1950's feel so don't book here expecting to get something newly renovated with latest furnishing and appliances. I didn't really expect this anyway but you get the feeling the owner is trying to maximize profits instead of reinvesting back into the rooms and the staff is trying to do these little extra things to make up for it. (You can rennovate while still retaining that old-school charm.) Many may characterize the rooms as having a nostalgic feel and the overall hotel having a boutique feel, which it does, and we liked that feel.The pool is small, but adequate. There is no Jacuzzi (a big minus). The layout of the hotel against the side of a hill with a U shape is great as it makes the inner courtyard/pool area shielded from the loud traffic of the busy street out front. Housekeeping service is excellent.I'd recommend staying here but don't go here with high expectations like you'll being staying at a small, boutique version of the Beverly Hills Hotel. I'm guessing that this place receives very high marks partially because comparatively it offers an excellent value for it's location and especially for those that prefer an alternative to the high-rise hotel experience.  
<Date>Apr 14, 2007

<Author>DharmaGirl
<Content>Second stay at the Magic Castle Hotel I loved this place so much the first time I stayed back in October, that I booked it again for the night of February 3rd.I'd requested the same 1-bdrm I'd had the last time, but they put me in a room that was actually bigger and nicer than the first one! (The bathroom in this one was especially roomy.)Reception was great about getting me checked in quickly since I was exhausted and needed a nap!Again, the sound of soft music was playing as I first entered the room. I should say apartment instead of room since the suite is enormous, with a hallway leading from the large living room to the bathroom, and then another to the bedroom. Just incredibly big for a hotel room!I was going to a comedy club on Hollywood Blvd, and instead of calling a cab in the nightmare Saturday night traffic I was advised by the hotel staff to walk where I was going instead, so I did. That was just perfect. I walked up the bustling boulevard over all the stars on the sidewalk and watched the tourists gawk at the familiar Hollywood landmarks and street performers. It was about a 10 minute brisk walk and well worth it.I got back to the hotel earlier than I'd expected that night, so I went down to the desk for snacks (complimentary) like candy bars and microwave popcorn. I was even able to check out a DVD for the night, free. (There's a DVD player in the full entertainment center in the large living room.) Since it was still fairly early and the hotel shuttle driver was on the site I asked if they could take me up the hill to their sister property, the Hollywood Hills Hotel. (It's on the grounds of the restaurant Yamashiro.) The view of all of Los Angeles and Hollywood from up there was just phenomenal. Evidently, the rooms aren't as nice as in the Magic Castle Hotel, but the views more than make up for it. (No views from the Magic Castle Hotel down the hill.)Afterward, I made my microwave popcorn and a cup of tea in my large full kitchen, and sat out on my big balcony overlooking the pool and just enjoyed the quiet night and the great weather.Overall, another great stay. Management and all the front desk employees went above and beyond to make my stay comfortable and get me everything I needed. I'll definitely be staying here again the next time I go to Hollywood.

<Author>emkel98
<Content>Affordable near Hollywood attractions I have stayed with my family at the Magic Castle three times over the course of the past year. Although parking ($9) is not included in the rate, when you factor in the free continental breakfast (way above average pastries), it's an excellent bargain. The kitchen is equipped with the basics. The heated pool is well-maintained. The front-desk staff is very helpful. The rooms are slightly dated and there are some stains/wear on the furniture. I'm a neat freak and the cleanliness of the room - while fine for my husband - leaves a bit to be desired. This is a great hotel for families and the neighborhood is certainly safe enough to walk in - just two blocks to the Walk of Fame.
