<Author>Richchick
<Content>A fantastic find in Hollywood! I just returned from a 5 day stay in Hollywood with my 2 teenagers ages 13  16. We have enjoyed staying in many 5 star hotels around the world and have experienced very good service. I have to say that the Magic Castle Hotel can stand with the best when it comes to friendly staff, great service, and cleanliness.Arrival:The hotel is centrally located in Hollywood and was easy to find.The lobby is not large but is very accommodating, welcoming and tastefully decorated. The staff greeted us warmly and seemed genuinely friendly. On one side of the lobby there was a large arrangement of cookies, an assortment of teas, spiced cider, and packets for hot chocolate. There was also cool water containing sliced cucumbers.A delicious continental breakfast is served every morning from 7- 10AM. The food is arranged in the lobby and can be enjoyed out by the pool or you can take it to your room.Checking in was quick and the staff carried our luggage to our room which was on the second level. There are no elevators but there are rooms on the ground level if stairs are a challenge. There are also a few steps to the front entrance of the hotel.The rooms surround a large, lovely courtyard. Many of the rooms on the second and third levels have balconys overlooking the courtyard. Ours did not but I will know to ask ahead for one next time we visit.In the center of the courtyard is a 'splash pool'. If you want Olympic laps this is not the pool for you. It is just the right size for a refreshing dip and floating around. My kids loved it.Our room:We had the junior suite and found it to be fairly large and very clean. The carpeting looked new.In addition to the TV there was a DVD player and CD player. My kids brought their laptops and there was wirless internet for them.The hotel has a nice complimentay DVD library. When my kids went to select DVDs they were surprised with a complimentary bucket of microwave popcorn packets and an assortment of candy. The beds have down comforters and the mattresses were firm and comfortable. Turndown service is provided every evening along with chocolate mints.Location:The hotel is located at the foot of a hill within 2 blocks of busy Hollywood Blvd. Once you turn off of Hollywood Blvd the crowds and noise seem to thin out appreciably.The subway is about 3 blocks from the hotel on Hollywood Blvd and we used it to get to Universal Studios. The city was in preparation for the Oscars while we were there. All of these preparations take place in the 2 block area close to the hotel. The Hollywood/ Highland subway stop is closed on the day of the Oscars. Metro and auto traffic is detoured as well beginning several days before the Oscar presentations. Pedestrian traffic is also detoured on Hollywood Blvd beginning several days prior to Oscar day but all the major sights are still accessible such as the Kodak theater, walk of fame, and Chinese theater. I was told that this inconvenience only happens during the week of Oscar preparations every year. We found it fun and exciting to watch the city get ready for the Oscars day by day despite the inconvenience of the detours.Staff:I have never been treated better at any hotel that I have ever stayed at. The staff just go out of their way to make your stay pleasant and enjoyable. They are friendly, courteous and they let you know that they are there for you. When my kids were up into the night with jet lag I spent lots of time going to the lobby for DVD's and snacks and Marzia on the night shift was so patient and helpful. All the staff should be commended.They give you 5 star service and 5 star treatment. There are lots of bigger, grander, more luxurious hotels in L.A. but the staff at the Magic Castle make it stand along side any of them. In my opinion, there is none better.We enjoyed our stay at the Magic Castle Hotel and highly recommend it.  
<Date>Feb 24, 2007

<Author>rag714
<Content>Great Place to Stay We adored the Magic Castle. It was a real delight to find such clean, comfortable, friendly and quiet accommodations just a block away from the madness of Hollywood Boulevard. From the moment we arrived (and were upgraded to a suite) until we checked out we could find nothing to fault. Our only minor quibble is that our suite was on the back with a view of a wall. However, since we were receiving a spacious suite for the price of a standard room it would have been ungracious to complain. The hotel胁's leek decor, the spacious rooms (at least the suites; we didn't see the standard rooms) the delightful courtyard, and the excellent continental breakfasts (pastries from Susina's Bakery are terrific!) have been mentioned in other reviews and we concur with all of the positive comments. Worthy of special mention is the outstanding staff. Everyone was very friendly, helpful and knowledgeable of the area. Thanks to Nick and Sean (spelling?) for all your good advice and the drinks and snacks!  By the way, one of the best reasons for staying here is to gain access to the Magic Castle Club. The only way you can get in to see the magic shows is to be a member of the Academy of Magical Arts or to stay at the hotel. The Victorian building in which the Club is located is a real hoot, dinner was good, and the magic shows were absolutely terrific.

<Author>cmmb2005
<Content>Sweet, caring staff and a pleasant stay I am a single mother with three children. We stayed at The Magic Castle hotel on 1/4/07 and 1/5/07. I had a Jr. Suite with a kitchen.There were a few minor issues which are easy to overlook. In the bathroom, the paint was peeling a bit on the ceiling, and the shower looked a bit worn. This hotel does not boast to be a 4-star, but it is clean, courteous and great for families and those not expecting a hotel of a Four Seasons caliber. This is a nicely run, boutique hotel with an outstanding staff! During that time, I found the staff to be genuine in their offerings of help with luggage, suggestions for dinner and giving directions. My daughter became ill during our trip, and the front desk was quick to help with names and phone numbers of the local pharmacies in the area. They later asked about her and how she was feeling. They also wanted to know how we liked their suggestions for dinner. This staff is the friendliest, most courteous staff I've ever seen. If a guest has problems with this hotel, it is most likely the guest who is being difficult, not the staff.The breakfast was well above the rest, and was put out promptly and well stocked. That breakfast surpasses all the other hotels I've stayed at. The beds and pillows were soft and inviting, and the rooms were large.This was a perfect stay for my family and the kids and I will certainly be back. The location is great...walking distance from everything we had planned to see. The neighborhood was fine. I felt safe there, even walking at night. Next time we come, we'll definitely take advantage of the Sunday Brunch at the Castle. Sorry we missed it. Thanks Magic Castle! Keep up the good work.

<Author>kathymander
<Content>Magical stay We have just returned from a 5 night stay over the New Year's Holiday at the Magic Castle Hotel in Hollywood. The staff were great and even provide a ride up to the Yamashiro Restaurant at the top of the hill above the Hotel. The view and food are incredible. Memoirs of a Geisha was partly filmed here. The hotel staff were very friendly and accomodating. Walked into the lobby to the wonderful smell of hot cider and cinnamon(cookies too). Afternoon tea is available every day. Bottled water is provided as you need it. Our room was spacious for our family of 4: 2 adults and 2 teenagers. We could fall asleep in our bedroom and not hear their late night movie.Had a full kitchen. Every morning we took our breakfast back to our room to sit on the patio enjoying the morning sun. Breakfast was great, cereal, pastries, fruit, yogurt, granola, juices, coffee. There is a pleasant heated outdoor pool for sunning or swimming. Staff helped us with directions/maps and reservations. We did the family brunch at the Magic Castle Club on Sunday at their recommendation. We had great food and were treated to a Magic show that was funny and truly amazing. Our son thought it was as good as Universal Studios. This hotel is located very close(walking distance) to Grauman's Chinese Theatre and the stars walk on Hollywood Boulevard. We took the metro to Universal Studios-it is 1 stop away. We were centrally located to make easy drives of 20 or 30 min to Pasadena, Santa Monica and the Getty Center. We will definitely stay here when we come back to LA. This hotel helped make our vacation an almost perfect trip.

<Content>Had a magic birthday at the Magic Castle Hotel... I had wanted to go to the Magic Castle Club for my birthday but heard that it was a private club for members only. However, my boyfriend discovered that guests of this hotel were given admission to the club during their stay. The reviews looked good so we took a chance. We were not disappointed. The staff was extremely friendly and accommodating. Upon arrival we were offered cookies and hot cider. The club is just right next door to the hotel, but if you ask, they are happy to shuttle you up the small hill just so the ladies don't have to try and hoof it up there in high heels! I certainly appreciated that. :-)When we came back from the Magic Castle (which we LOVED!) there was a pretty box all wrapped up in a ribbon that contained an adorable mini birthday cake and a card signed by the staff! What a nice touch--and yummy cake too.We were surprised to hear that the pool is heated to 80 degrees year round so we took advantage of that fact and had a romantic and refreshing moonlight swim. (They don't close the pool at night, they just ask that you observe quiet hours and not disturb others).The hotel was close enough to walk to all the other places that we wanted to see so it was the perfect place to stay. I would definitely stay there again if I am in the area. Thanks Magic Castle Hotel Staff for a magic birthday!

<Author>SydneyTravellers
<Content>Great stay at the Magic Castle Our family of four stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel for two nights after a long flight from Sydney. The staff were extremely helpful in booking us a Hollywood tour at short notice and accomodated our every need throughout our stay. The room (a one bedroom unit) we stayed in was bright and clean, just next to the pool. The breakfast was plentiful and it was nice to be able to take your choices back to your room. The location of the hotel is great, we got the train easily to Universal studios (a great day). Be aware that Hollywood Bvld is pretty sleazy at night, and there are many homeless people living in the park across the road from the hotel. The staff suggested Micalo's for dinner one night, a short walk from the hotel. This is a wonderful restaurant with singing waitors.We booked this hotel due to the favourable reviews in Tripadvisor and were not disappointed.

<Content>Service was great, but room just ok We stayed here for a night while visiting friends and family. The staff couldn't have been nicer- from the glass of limonada when we arrived to great directions on our way out to dinner and complimentary scones, fruit, and juice for breakfast. Turndown service was a nice touch, though, and the pillows were really plushy.For us, the location, $8 parking, and service stood out above everything else, and if you're looking for some charm in Hollywood, this is the place to go.

<Author>TimPithers
<Content>Fantastic location, great staff The Magic Castle Hotel is right in the middle of Hollywood - you can't beat the location! It's about 2 minutes walk from the Walk of Fame, Grauman's Chinese Theatre etc. This was fantastic for our 5 night stay as it put us in a perfect location from which to explore everything we had set out to. The hotel's staff is probably it's greatest asset, as all of the members are very friendly, welcoming and incresibly helpful. Our suite was spacious and comfortable but quite dark and hot. I guess that was due to it being a ground floor room. The air conditioners worked fine, if a little noisy. Maybe a 1st floor room would be better. The DVD player and CD player are nice additions as is the DVD collection available at the front desk. I think the hotel would benefit from a lick of paint, especially around the pool area, but this didn't spoil the enjoyment of our stay. We really enjoyed the breakfast buffet (delicious croissants) as it was a nice relaxing start to the day. We took up the offer available to hotel guests to visit the Magic Castle Club next door which proved to be an enjoyable evening of dining and magic. The interior of the building is amazing!

<Author>MissRyan
<Content>Can't recommend it enough! My boyfriend and I booked a double room at the Magic Castle, for our week long trip to LA in June 06.When we arrived we found we had a *huge* suite. The staff were absolutely lovely, friendly and funny and very attentive. It had a great pool, a laundry room, and tasty breakfast was available every morning.The suite was great, complete with a good sized kitchen and balcony. The only slight let down was the bathroom, which could have done with a lick of paint, and the carpets could have done with a bit of a clean, but generally it was excellent, and extremely good value for money.The customer service at the hotel was really good, they left Hersheys kisses next to the bed every day, and in the evenings left us a card with the next days weather forecast on so that we'd be prepaped. The staff always had time to listen to you, and were full of suggestions and recommendations.The hotel is in a great location, just next to the walk of fame, right in the centre of Hollywood. I really can't recommend it enough.One night we went for dinner at the Magic Castle club, which is next door, and while it is a beautiful building, and the magic shows were spectacular, the food was overpriced and not very nice. I'd recommend going for the shows, but definitely not for dinner.

<Author>Proboscus
<Content>The Best Ever This hotel is amazing. It is a small old fashioned boutique hotel with the best of everything - not in terms of glitz and glamour - in terms of the things that really matter. The suites are roomy, modern, clean, and comfortable and have every amenity you need. The beds were great too! There was enough room to stay for weeks; in fact it was like a small apartment. The pool and layout of the hotel is perfect and makes you feel like you are in a community. The location is great if you want to walk around Hollywood and do the tourist stuff. Walk up to the Hollywood Bowl and see the museum there. It's interesting. The unique and plentiful breakfast was delicious and great way to start the day - sitting at the pool and eating fresh baked goodies. There is parking under the hotel for a reasonable price and it is easy. But the absolute best thing about this hotel hands down is the staff. From the minute I spoke to Gretchen on the phone to book the room until the second we said we left and Mike and his staff said goodbye - all of them were amazing! They deserve a customer service award. Even my two teenage boys could not get over how helpful the staff was about everything. And always pleasant with a smile and a friendly attitude. As my boys put it  Mike is the Man. They were very impressed. Oh yes, and don't miss the view from the restaurant on top of the hill above the Castle - also one of their properties. The food was great there too! I would go back to LA just to stay at the Castle again. Enjoy!!

<Content>A Magical stay My son and I stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel during a vacation to the LA area. The hotel is small but in a great location, just two blocks from Hollywood Blvd. One of the best parts was its association with the Magic Castle. Minors can't get into the Castle to see the performances except on weekend brunches and unless you are with a member. The only exception is for those staying at the hotel. Since my son is a magic buff, that was a big attraction of staying there.However, we were pleasantly surprised with just about everything. Most impressive was the staff which was so incredibly friendly and helpful. They were never overbearing but always willing to help out.The rooms were decent, but not overly impressive. They had everything we needed. I was a little taken aback by the carpets, which looked a little worn, but half-way through our stay, they were being replaced. The beds were very comfy while the bathrooms were a little tired, but still very functional and clean.Every morning there was a continental breakfast served in the small lobby. I ususally took my food out to the pool-side tables and sat there. The pool was a great feature; it wasn't too big but was great for cooling off. My only complaint was one night, at about 2 a.m., some drunks jumped in and were a little noisy. But that was an isolated occurence.If you're there on vacation, you can easily walk to Hollywood Blvd and all the attractions there. As well, the hotel next door -- which I wouldn't suggest you stay at -- is where Janis Joplin was found dead.Overall, I'd go back to this hotel in a minute, based largely on the staff. Great job

<Author>Vienna81
<Content>Great value We stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel for four nights in early August, and we really enjoyed this hotel. Everyone who works in the hotel is very friendly and helpful, especially with providing recommendations on places to eat and helping out with directions. We stayed in a studio room and the furniture was renovated, but the carpet was not. The bed was large and comfortable. The hotel is a few blocks from all the Hollywood attractions like Kodak Theatre, etc. The breakfast is basic and pretty good. We liked the free DVD rentals a lot. There is a fridge in the studio.There was that there was a lot of noise the first two nights from other hotel guests next door. The walls are very thin. There were some cracks in the wall. Also, the shower temperature was not totally consistent. The parking garage is good but small, and the spaces are very tight. We did not use the wireless internet, so we cannot comment on it. There is an internet kiosk that is 20 cents/minute if you do not have a laptop.If you are looking for a posh and luxurious experience, this is not the hotel for you. However, if you are looking for great value and a comfortable experience, and don't plan on being on your room all day, Magic Castle is a good fit.

<Author>ChoosyPerson
<Content>Disappointed - not as we expected from reviews or Hotel website We use Tripadvisor for all our hotel choices when visiting a new city and as Magic Castle was rated #3 in Los Angeles and the Hotel's own website shows lovely photos of a hotel completely renovated in 2004 we booked with confidence.Apparently the ground floor consists of suites which are renovated, but the other rooms are certainly not renovated and are in fact quite shabby. The cleanliness was well below standard as the room was very dusty in all corners. Very old worn carpets, a functional but run down bathroom, a very noisy dilapidated air conditioning system and hard to control ceiling fan are among the highlights. On the plus side the room was a decent size, the bed was quite comfortable, there is an empty fridge which is useful and a desk, plus a large TV and a DVD player. The wardrobe is a fair size with large mirrors and a safe. On our last day we took the complimentary continental breakfast which was very good and we would have taken every day in hindsight, although there wasn't quite enough informal seating to accomodate all the guests wanting to sit outside. We found the staff to be varied - some were helpful when we asked for advice. However there was a general reluctance to change our traveller's cheques each day which seemed incredible - we were often told they didn't have $100 to change, but then go back and ask someone else and they would. This is a small apartment style hotel, with the feel of a beach hotel without the beach. The very small pool is the focal point around which the three or four floors of rooms are built - with no ramps or elevators! Getting your cases up the stairs is a nightmare! The location of the hotel is it's best feature. Our main reason for visiting was to see a show at the Hollywood Bowl which turned out to be a 10-15 minute walk which saved being stuck in traffic. The Chinese Theatre and other main attractions are 5 minutes walk away. However, there are numerous other hotels situated along the same road which would be worth investigating if you wish to stay in this location.We would almost certainly not return to the Magic Castle hotel and would not recommend it to friends.  
<Date>Jul 19, 2006

We advised the hotel of the problem they assured us it would get fixed but it wasn't. By our second night stay, it didn't matter if we had three air conditioners running or only one, the breaker kept going off. When we checked out, the hotel staff advised us that they were aware of the problems in that specific room (106) and to compensate they gave us two nights of free parking. What we don't seem to understand is why would they accomodate us in the only room that had inadequate air conditionning and an old run down sofa bed when we purposely had advised them that one of the guests had a medical problem.

<Author>CatCalico
<Content>An Enjoyable Visit We stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel on June 2nd and June 3rd. There were five of us traveling (3 adults and 2 kids ages 9 and 11) and we stayed in a one bedroom suite. Upon check-in we were greeted by the staff at the front door. The person at the desk was very pleasant and helpful and made us feel like we were valued guests. After we checked in we were moving our luggage from the car to our room. When a staff member saw us moving our luggage, he immediately offered to assist us. Our room was spacious and comfortable. We requested a roll-away bed when we made our reservations and it was in the room when we checked in. The weather was quite hot during our stay and the room was pleasantly cool. There was an air conditioner in the living room and bedroom. The kids wanted to use the pool immediately and it was quite refreshing. The breakfast provided in the lobby area was really good with a variety of fruit and freshly baked goodies. The coffee was very tasty as well. The location was great - walking distance to the Chinese Theater and Walk of Fame. We were able to go to the Sunday Brunch at the Magic Castle which was really nice. Our stay was enjoyable. The staff at this Hotel really knows how to provide an exceptional cutomer experience. The entire staff from the manager at the front desk to the housekeeping staff work in conjuction to make the guest feel special. We all had a great time - it was a nice break from the average chain hotel.

<Content>Very Good Choice for LA Stayed with a TV crew at the Magic Castle, and although I suffered many jokes about wanting to stay at a hotel with such an odd name it turned out to be a great spot. LA is tough for hotels - so much of the city is not a city, at least by non-LA standards - it's hard to find a place where you can actually walk to a store or restaurant. The Magic Castle - which seems off of a set for a TV show or film - is well located, friendly (in the best sense of the word) and comfortable. If you get a suite it's really a one bedroom apartment - some of the small rooms, however, can be quite small. Rates vary according to season - but most of the year it's quite affordable. There is no elevator - which would have been a problem except that the staff lent a hand and even with a lot of metal boxes we were okay.Jon - Montreal, Quebec

<Author>bridge65
<Content>Stay here - its great We stayed here for 14 days in April 06. Had a one bedroom suite which had a very comfortable sofa bed in the loungeroom for our daughter. The location is excellent being very close to Hollywood Bvde. There is also a store there to buy your groceries/provisions etc. The staff are excellent - nothing too much trouble, and the housekeeping was very thorough. DON'T stay in a hotel, boxed into a confining air conditioned room - stay here and enjoy the balcony, fresh air, kitchen and comfortable furniture. The beds are excellent and the pillows a dream. There is a laundry with cheap washing/drying facilities - a necessity for a longer stay. Internet too. A light breakfast is also served. The train to get you to Universal Studios is very close. Walk up to the Japanese restaurant just behind the hotel for a terrific view. If you go to the Magic Show at the Castle, gentlemen need a tie and jacket. We went to some very nice restaurants only a $10-$15 US ride away. The taxi from LAX is about $45-$50 US. So we highly recommend this as very good value for money for those people who want a bit of room around them, above average service and good location in Hollywood area. Thank you to ALL the staff for making our stay so enjoyable and comfortable. The Andersons, NSW, Australia.

It's not a high-end hotel; however, all the above mentioned things madeup for the lack of posh. I would drefinitely stay there again.

<Author>MercerIslandMom
<Content>Great Hotel Staff - Avoid Suite 222 At All Costs This review would have 2 stars if not for the staff. I researched Hollywood hotels for quite a while, and loved Magic Castle's spacious 2 bedroom site with the hip, new furniture displayed on the Magic Castle's website. Our family arrived and was ushered to Suite 222, the one room outside the hotel which was a (recently?) converted studio. It was dingy, had only 1 of the 2 promised bathrooms, offered closets so musty that I immediately re-closed the doors, and a shower the size of a coffin. But the real horrible twist was the paper-thin walls and the loud noise from the street. I immediately requested a room change but none was available and the newbie clerk said just close the windows. With all windows closed, this heavy sleeper was awoken multiple times and finally crawled into bed with her children in an inner room where noise was still heard.I went to the clerk the next morning almost in tears: for $250 a night, I expected more, at least a decent night of sleep. She ended up refunding the night's charge, assigning us to a new room (switching us with new unfortunate guests), and treated us to a box of treats. Very pleasant. The new room was all that I had expected: light, roomy, and hip. No street noise since we were in a courtyard off the street. It was recently renovated but already wear was showing through, but still, after that nightmare Suite 222, it was heaven.Great staff. Ready, helpful, and pleasant.

<Author>tru205
<Content>Spacious Apartment Like Hotel in Hollywood We have just returned from a three week trip to the US where our final port of call was L.A. We drove into LA (having hired a car in Anaheim), saw the Hollywood sign up on the hill and exited the 101 freeway to cruise along a dirty and dumpy street that is Sunset Boulevard. Despite the imagery its name conjures up, Hollywood in reality holds minimal glitz or glamour and as we neared the hotel, we started to worry that our hotel may be similar to the surroundings.But no! We were pleasantly surprised as we rounded the corner to the Magic Castle Hotel and were suitably impressed - it was a fabulous place to stay. For the great price it offered location, space and amenities with only a couple of shortcomings.The hotel appears to be an old apartment block remodelled into a hotel. The rooms all surround a pool (very Melrose Place like) and are very spacious. Our room had a full kitchen with microwave, stove, fridge and dining table. There was a fold out sofa bed in the second room for our son. (Great for kids but not really for adults as it was not all that comfortable.) There was a television in both rooms (though the one in the master bedroom would only show one channel), a dvd player (you could borrow dvds from reception at no charge) and the bathroom had a bath and shower but was a little tired. The room itself was not young, but was spotless and there were some very nice little touches including chocolates on pillows, a card with the expected weather for the next day and a complimentary continental breakfast. The bed in the master bedroom was incredibly comfortable! The staff were very friendly and helpful, the security was good and undercover, secure parking was available for $8 a day. The hotel was located a block away from the Chinese Theatre and the stars in the sidewalk of Hollywood Boulevard - but LA is somewhere you really need a car so depending on what you are interested in this would determine whether you thought it was a good location.Overall, a great hotel for the price. A fabulous option for travellers with kids as you can cook for yourself and have the space and a pool to amuse the children. Highly recommend!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Had a wonderful stay at the Magic Castle We just returned from April spring break in Hollywood with our two teenagers, and we loved our four nights at the Magic Castle Hotel. First and foremost is the service at the hotel. It is rated as a two star place, but that doesn't do justice to the very customer-focused attitude of all the staff. They helped us whenever we needed it, and they treated us with a sincere friendliness that you don't learn in customer service class. It seems that the owners or managers have done a great job of hiring the right people. They all seemed genuinely concerned about our happiness at the hotel, and they went out of their way to help us whenever necessary. Again, this wasn't the false smile, patronizing attitude pretense that seems to pass for customer service; this was a bunch of nice people trying to make sure we had a good time at their place.One example: Our key card was not working for us to enter their garage, so one of the staff members came out of the hotel to help. (Yes, apparently they were monitoring the garage entrance and noticed our problem.) When I pointed out the problem, the gentleman used his card to open the garage for us, then said that he would run inside, re-program my key card, and meet me in the garage to give me my card. (Yes, he came down to meet me.) This is just one example of how they went out of their way to take care of us.We also enjoyed the other aspects of the hotel: the location is great (close proximity to all of the Hollywood attractions), our 1-bedroom suite was spacious and decorated with personality (not a generic hotel look), and the heated pool, although on the small side, gave us a peaceful retreat from sightseeing (my kids loved the pool).We had a great time at the hotel and would stay there again in a heartbeat.

<Author>Tony_No
<Content>Great value for families at the price It all depends what you expect. If you are expecting a 4 * hotel you may be disappointed. If, like us, you are looking for pleasant spacious accomodation for a family of 4 you'll be very pleased. I thought it was great value for money. We stayed for 4 nights in an enormous 1 bed suite with 2 small children (5 and 7) sleeping on the lounge sofabed. The suite appeared to be a converted apartment and was very large and airy and nicely decorated in a light, modern style with new furniture and carpets (laid 2 days previously I was told). It was spotlessly clean. Our suite included a fully equipped kitchen . The kitchen appliances and wall cupboards, while freshly painted, are quite old, probably dating back to when the place was an apartment... The refurb budget clearly didn't stretch to ripping out all the old fixtures. An upside of having the old wall cupboards dotted around the suite was huge amounts of storage for luggage. The bedroom and bathroom were fine.The continental breakfast was very good and the service excellent. I don't think I've ever had a better welcome from any hotel than the one that we got when we checked in. All of the staff (Front desk, security, cleaning) are very helpful and take pride in the place.Pool was also fine and parking is available on the property for $5 per day. The location is very convenient for some of the tourist sites and there are plenty of places to eat within 10 minutes walk. We could hear traffic noise from our bedroom at night but it didn't stop us sleeping. I'd definitely recommend this place for families. In value for money terms it comes out as excellent, hence the rating here, even if in absolute terms it is not the Four Seasons.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Location and Very Spacious accommodation We recently stayed at the Magic Castle hotel with our two teenagers and had a 2 bedroom suite. The suite was apartment style newly remodelled, with large king bedrooms, bathroom, large lounge and full kitchen. Beds were very comfortable and bedding was good quality. The remodelling has definitely been done on a tight budget. New kitchen and beds but old carpet and living room furniture. Bathroom had new toilet and vanity but old bath with repainted rather than replaced tiling. Great to have a kitchen but only cooking utensil provided was a milk pan so couldnt really prepare a meal so still ate out every night.Reception staff were very helpful and friendly. Even though the weather was cool and wet for April our boys used the heated pool every evening. Breakfast was OK but you have to eat outside or in your room. It was very wet during our stay and we had to carry trays of food through the rain and up many steps to our room.If travelling with the family we would definitely stay here again for its good value, spacious and clean accommodation and its great location, but if we were without the kids we'd probably look for somewhere a little more upscale.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Okay...not great We recently spent 5 days at the Magic Castle, encouraged by the reviews here. Overall, it was an okay experience, but not great.The plusses: The rooms are quite large. Our one bedroom suite was clean and the full kitchen was nice to have. I cannot compliment the housekeeping staff enough. Also Ashley at the front dest was very helpful and pleasant. Location is good-- it is within walking distance to the Hollywood and Highland entertainment complex and most of the other Hollywood attractions. It is also one stop down from Universal Studios on the Metro. The adequate: There is a continental breakfast. If you love carbs, this is the place for you! There were only pastries, cereal, and juice available. The not so great: The hotel, being on a busy street can be noisy. The quieter rooms were off street, but up lots of stairs. If you have bad knees, or are not in good shape you WILL be exhausted! In short either you deal with the noise or you get put in a room far away with no elevator in sight.

<Author>arlenejoe
<Content>Many amenities and great value This is a fine location in Hollywood - 1 block from Grauman's Chinese Theater and the whole tourist scene on that same block. Good eating, lots of movie theaters, shopping, fun stuff happening all along the sidewalk, stars and handprints of celebrities. Yet, the hotel itself feels residential. In fact, the hotel was an apartment complex before, so the feel is very homey around the swimming pool. Service is the best - friendly, quick to fix the shower door, very responsive. They certainly aim to please. Yamashiro's, the famous upscale restaurant in the gorgeously historic building overlooking the city, is part of the business, so they booked our dinner reservation and drove us up to the restaurant. Best part is that the hotel stay allows us entry into the Members Only Magic Castle. We had Sunday brunch there with our kids and saw 3 shows. Very fun afternoon that lasts 3 hours.The price is a real bargain for what you get. Don't expect a physically sparkling site - it's an older building that's been remodeled nicely but not extravagently. The only downside is the noise. Pretty noisy, especially with the cheerleading team that was in town for a competition. We probably wouldn't stay there again because we wouldn't need to be in that location and see the magic shows or dine at Yamashiro's again, but for a one-time treat, I'd highly recommend it!

<Author>BLGAW
<Content>Nice Hotel We were a group of 5 (parents, 2 teens and a grandmother) that stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel March 11-14. The hotel is located at the bottom of a hill, next door to the Magic Castle Club. My mother and I would walk up the hill to the Japanese restaurant (Yamashiro's) at the top to enjoy the view each morning. The location is very good for just walking to the Kodak Theater or Graumanns Chinese Theater. Since we had a car, it was also centrally located to everything else.Our one bedroom unit was always clean. The furnishings were kind of art deco simple. We also had a small kitchen with stove and refrigerator.The staff was awesome!! They could answer any question about Los Angeles and always did it with a smile and additional information that I would not have thought to ask. (I am wondering if they have to take some kind of knowledge test before they are hired?) They were always very accomodating and quick to bring extra towels or blankets when we asked. Since the weather was chillier than we had expected, we did not use the pool. But our daughters are hoping to come back during the summer. We would definitely stay here again.

<Author>nls1330
<Content>Not as "magical" as we hoped! We spent two February nights at The Magic Castle based on Trip Advisor reviews. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great service, good hotel for families with young children My husband, 2-year old son and I went to LA last weekend to visit my sister-in-law, and we stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel overnight, based on the recommendations I had read on this site. I was very pleased to find we agreed with the very positive comments. Our room was spacious, tidy, and well-equipped (e.g., kitchen has eat-in area with table/chairs for 4 and comes with dishes, glasses, dishwashing soap; plenty of towels; 2 plush bathrobes), and with the pull-out couch in the living room, we were able to let our son go to sleep early in the bedroom while my husband and I stayed up watching television and relaxing in the living room. The staff was warm, helpful, and accomodating. When we called to ask for recommendations on take-out/delivery in the area, they brought menus to our room. We later called to inquire about drink vending machines, and sodas were brought to our door. The following morning, we found the continental breakfast options to be ample, and of much better quality than you find at many chain hotels. The only glitch we encountered was a lapse in hot water, which we were told was a problem the hotel was having, and that was remedied within a few hours. I should also note that travelers keep in mind that this is a 2-star hotel--there won't be a *wow* factor upon entering the hotel, and there are certain signs of use (e.g., bleach stain on the sofa, chipped pain on the molding) that you wouldn't encounter at, say, a Ritz Carlton. But bearing that in mind, I felt the hotel was a very good value and the excellent customer service can't be beaten--we would certainly stay there again the next time we are in town.

<Author>newmansgang
<Content>Hospitality, Hospitality, Hospitality I booked six rooms for myself and colleagues for a stay in Hollywood to attend a teacher's conference. I did this after consulting Tripadvisor, and I'd have to say that our experience was even better than the reviews. Darren, the Hotel Manager did his best to make us happy from booking through check-out. In fact, I left my luggage at the hotel and did not realize that it remained behind at the hotel. We were already at the airport, and it was too late to return to the hotel. After a call, Darren saved the day by delivering the bag to the airport himself-on his day off! The rooms were spacious, clean, and the bed was firm and like sleeping in my own. All of the desk personnel were friendly, concerned and consistently helpful(including shawn, ashley, gretchen, jason and stan). These people are so good at what they do that they should open a hospitality management school. The breakfast was very, very good -scones, croissants, wolfgang puck coffee, cereals and fresh fruit. We have traveled quite a bit (around the world), and I must say that this establishment is one of the best values out there. So, if you're planning a stay in Hollywood, strongly consider the Magic Castle!

<Author>Hollybear
<Content>Sensational service My family spent 3 nights in a Magic Castle self-contained suite in October 2005. From the moment we got there the staff were incredibly friendly, helpful, intelligent and funny, and this made our stay there an absolute delight. I chose this place for the price and because of the comments made on this website by other travellers who were so impressed with the service. The 2-bedroom suite more than met our needs (including 3 TV's, which set the kids in raptures!). The suites look out over the pool - most of the suites have balconies as well - and it was just a lovely cosy atmosphere. While we were loafing around the pool we were offered towels, free bottled water and even icy-poles! Breakfast is included in the price and consists of a good selection of cereals and juices, together with great coffee and fresh cakes and pastries. You can eat by the pool or take it back to your room while you read the complementary paper. As well as being terrific value for money, the location is excellent; one block from Hollywood Boulevard and one metro stop from Universal Studios. All the hotel staff were friendly and helpful, always. I have never stayed in a hotel where everybody was so good-humoured. On our last day we left our bags at reception before flying out later that day, and I was wondering what to do with a pair of Mickey Mouse ears that would probably get scrunched in transit. When we came back to collect our bags, Gretchen (front desk) had packed them in a separate box, with 2 polaroid photos of her and the office manager Mike modelling the ears. How cool is that!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Won't stay anywhere else My sisters and I stayed at the Magic Castle for our Hollywood getaway weekend after reading the reviews for it on the internet. We loved it and will not stay anywhere else if we ever get back to Hollywood. Mike Filson really knows how to pick his staff, as every person who worked there was friendly, helpful, and willing to do whatever it took to make our stay pleasurable. They took the time to counsel us on where to go, how to get there, and even helped us get the transportation we needed.  The rooms were spacious, and although the bathrooms were a little older, we never found that to be a problem. For those who like to cook, there is a kitchen in every room.  The hotel is within walking distance of Hollywood Boulevard and all the attractions there. We took taxis wherever we went, and rented a car for one day.  I highly recommend this hotel, if for nothing else, the excellent service always with a smile.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fabulous Hotel! 5 Star Service! I have to admit, I was a bit weary when booking my room at the Magic Castle Hotel. I have read the reviews and made my decision based on them. I have checked out other hotels reviews, and decided that I liked the Magic Castle Hotel. I was glad I stayed there! From the first minute I checked in, I was treated like royalty. The manager was there to open the door for me, the lovely girl at the front desk offered me a complimentary bottled water at check in, and then they whisked me away to my room. On the way to the room, they told me about the hotel, informed me that the pool was open 24 hours. I have never heard of a hotel that has a 24 hour pool. I sure did enjoy those late night swims! The next morning I woke up and went to the lobby area to enjoy a wonderful continental breakfast. This is not your typical hotel breakfast. They served Wolfgang Puck coffee, fresh fruit, juices and cereal. You must try the scones and the criossants! Excellent! They even came to my table to refill my coffee! Later that day I approached the front desk on advice on what to do. They have tons of information on area attractions. Did I mention that they are one block from the world famous Chinese Theater and the new Kodak Theater? I was given information on local places to eat, museums and great tourist maps! So I went on a great walking tour of the city. It was nice! After a long day of walking and sightseeing, I came back to the hotel to find my bed turned down with a small chocolate kiss on my pillow. Of course, I went for my late night swim and called it a night! I often travel to LA for business and was happy to see that the hotel offers free high speed wireless. Its great to be able to work from my room or sit around the pool area. It was pretty warm when I visited, so I was offered popsicles! I thought this was playful and friendly! Every single staff member I came in contact with was ever so friendly. Always smiling and willing to help! They even remembered my name!! The room I got was spacious and lovely. Apparantly it wasn't one of the newly remodeled rooms, but I still loved it. New furnishings and a great bed! My room had a balcony that overlooked the pool. I suggest you make that request when you are making your reservations! I can go on and on about this wonderful hotel! I have read some of the negative comments from other guests, but I didn't see any of that happening. Yes the hotel is on a busy street, but the noise isn't that bad. I did hear the people next to me, but it wasn't a major deal to me. I can't wait to go back! I feel like family there! Keep up the good work! A big thanks to Ashley and Mike who gave me great directions and information on things to do. To all of you reading this post, book your room here! You won't be dissatisfied!!

<Author>DavidLau
<Content>Good Service but Noisy location We stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel for 3 nights in October 2005. The reason that we picked this hotel was to have a kitchen and be close to our destination - Universal Studios. As previously stated in all of the other reviews, the crown jewel of this hotel is the very good service given by the young staff. Also previously stated, the layout of the hotel is as the set of the Melrose Place TV show. All of the rooms surround a small courtyard with a small pool in the middle. No elevators, just stairways. The rooms themselves are reasonably sized for a suite-type hotel. They have been recently renovated, but not particularly well. In our room, the bathroom door didn't shut properly and the baseboards were already peeling. The kitchen was fully stocked with pots, pans, utensils, etc. Besides the TVs, there was also a small stereo system in the living room and a DVD player - nice. The sofa bed was not comfortable as the mattress wasn't well supported to the metal frame. A nice feature is that they use down comforters instead of regular blankets. Of special note, was the great water pressure in the shower. It was like standing underneath a giant waterfall!The continental breakfast is good, not great. As previously mentioned the baked goods were above average. Parking is $8/day for the small gated garage. The garage is a little tight, but we didn't have problems finding a spot every night. The main reason that I'm only giving an average rating was the level of night-time noise. The walls are pretty thin. Eventhough the location of our room was supposedly one of the more quiet sections, there was much traffic and weekend-partying noise until 2am. Of course, this isn't solely the hotel's fault, but rather the nature of their location - 1 block away from the night-life hub of Hollywood and Highland. On the plus side for the location:a) the hotel is a 4 minute walk from Grauman's Chinese theaterb) we took the metro to Universal Studios, which was another 2 minute walk from the Chinese theaterHere's an example of the good service: One of the female staff asked me if I slept well when I went to get breakfast and I complained about the noise. She purchased some ear plugs for us, and the plugs did help somewhat. In general, the staff is pretty attentive and helpful.For me, the good service and other perks didn't overcome the fact that it's an older building without good sound-proofing.  
<Date>Nov 5, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not Much to Fault It (But) I had chosen this hotel totally on the back of reading reviews on tripadvisor. When you are working to a budget, you want absolutely everything for the best price. I had asked for a view of the pool before our stay and the staff were lovely about this.. We had only booked a double which dont have balconies but they gave us the only room with a huge window overlooking the pool which looks lovely at night which is all I had really wanted having seen the pictures on the internet beforehand. We could just see the Club twinkling opposite above the other rooms. We were a bit unsure about how safe we were in LA so we decided to order takeaway to our room both nights. Despite asking lots of questions about how to go about this, the staff were always pleased to give advice and offer us menus to look at. I have to say that both meals were absolutely wonderful. I was a bit disappointed with the room I guess as it had no bedside lamps which meant that you had to get out of bed to turn the light off and also despite having items to make coffee, no coffee machine??? The thing which I found most difficult however was the noise. I am from the country in Lincolnshire and am used to quiet at night but there was a constant hum all of the time - we guessed from the pool. But on top of this, the fridge was also very loud and our neighbours decided it was a good idea to play their TV very loud until about 3 in the morning not considering other guests at all. This is of course our honest opinion and wouldn't want to put other people off from using what is a lovely hotel in a great location, with great staff and secure parking (small charge). Not it isn't 5 star but then it doesn't claim to be!!

<Author>VisitorTraveller
<Content>Definitely not a five star hotel We just got back from a three night stay at the Magic Castle. My feelings about this hotel are very mixed. On the one hand, the location was fantastic - it really IS one block behind Grauman's Chinese Theater, the Hollywood Walk of Fame, Hollywood Blvd, and very near the Hollywood Bowl.We paid over $1000 for three nights' stay. That included $8 a night parking and over $40 a night in taxes. I had told them on the phone that I was travelling with my mother who can't walk very well, and they said they'd do what they could but when we arrived we were put in the far outside building, up quite a lot of stairs. This required walking across a sloped and often slippery driveway as well as two flights of stairs. When we got to the room, it was huge, which was nice. Two separate bedrooms and an uncomfortable fold out couch in the living room (there were 3 of us), as well as a nice kitchen. But no balcony, no view of the pool, and the street we faced (Franklin) was NOISY - the traffic was horrendous, loud, constant honking and loud stereos until 3 in the morning every night. If you seal the windows and turn on the air conditioning it's tolerable but just barely. There was a musty smell to the room, and none of the remotes worked. Three tvs and not one remote worked. They did come up and fix that when we called down. The furnishings and carpet were serviceable but not as nice as the pictures on the website would lead you to believe. The breakfast was nice - Wolfgang Puck coffee and nice pastries, cereals and some little fruits. The staff is the best part of this hotel - friendly, helpful and very knowledgable. Shawn was the best, and Gretchen was nice too but they were very busy with what seemed to be more important guests than us, and we didn't feel particularly special.I would stay there again, but would demand better accomodations for the premium price we paid. If you want location, there's no better one for Hollywood. But if you want a quiet night's sleep there might be better places.  
<Date>Oct 25, 2005

<Content>Great staff, great location We stayed for 5 nights in October '05, and would definitely go back. Yes the bathroom in the suite we stayed in was a little in need of a refurb, yes you could hear the people above walking (or was it leaping?) across the floor, and the pipes are a little noisy, but the attitude of the staff and the location are unbeatable. Nothing is too much trouble for Jason, Gretchen, Sean and the rest of the crew.Having a kitchen is well worth it-there are a number of good supermarkets in the area, and dining in with a bottle of Californian wine-watching one of the many DVDs available free from reception-is a great way to finish a big day out. The staff can also recommend excellent pizza delivery. If you get the chance, go to the Magic Castle. We were a little sceptical, but had a great evening, and the food was much better than we were expecting. Overall a great introduction to LA.

<Author>cadgwith
<Content>Excellent hotel, location  Thank you to Tripadvisor users for your recommendations re this hotel - you were right. We stayed 7th to 11th September 2005, and it was great. I'd asked for a quiet room, on the top floor, with a bedroom away from the pool, but a balcony overlooking it, and that's exactly what I got (we were in room 215 - a suite). We had very little problem with noise - once a TV from next door could be heard through a connecting door, and some kids were in the pool late one evening - but, as our bedroom faced the back, and the connecting door led onto a hallway, not our bedroom, we were fine. The breakfast was good, the laundrette very cheap and convenient (with soap powder free!)  the lift up to Yamashiro much appreciated. The suite was large, effectively (if slightly noisily) air-conditioned and clean (with some charming original fitted furniture mixed with the modern items), and the bed big and comfortable. The staff were exceptional - very friendly, helpful in giving advice and booking taxis, restaurants, etc, and quick to mend a faulty safe in our room. The house keeping staff even did our washing up on 2 days. Yamashiro's was terrific - stunning views, a great atmosphere, and not too expensive. The hotel's location is very good - 5 minutes walk to Grauman's, 10 minutes to Hollywood and Highland metro station (and next door to the hotel where Janis Joplin died, rock fans). We felt safe walking around the area during the evening. We hope to return to LA, and if we do, we'd love to stay at the Magic Castle again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>The Magic Castle Hotel is Magical! My wife and I recently went to L.A. for a wedding and to visit our daughter. With all the rave reviews of the Magic Castle Hotel, how could we not try it? We arrived there in the evening with high expectations, but we were quickly disappointed. The carpeting in our room had numerous holes like cigarette burns (it turned out that these were dark spots). The next morning we debated about complaining to the management. After some hesitancy, we decided that management should know that our experience was not consistent with the reviews that we had read. After all, we were going to be there for three more nights. We started wondering whether the reviews were written by real guests of the hotel.We addressed the carpet problem with the person at the front desk. She was very understanding and offered to place us in another comparable room. However, this room was near the street, and we did not want to risk the possible noise. So we decided to stay put and thought that was the end of it.As we were enjoying our breakfast at poolside, we were approached by the general manager. He apologized and offered us further assistance. He indicated that another room was opening up that morning. A little later that morning he gave us the key for this newly vacated room. Were we surprised! The room was enormous with a full kitchen, dining area, living room, etc. Besides this free upgrade, he advised us that the first night would be deducted from our bill.With large smiles upon our faces, we promptly moved over our luggage to our new luxury suite. We then went back to the pool for swimming and sunbathing. Upon our return to the suite, we found a beautiful bouquet of flowers from a florest with a note apologizing for the inconvenience from the general manager. This was astonishing! Where do you get such service from a hotel?The remainder of our stay there could not have been better. The location is 2 blocks from Grauman's Theater and other tourist sites, as well as the subway that we took to Olvera St. The pool was refreshing with staff members bringing out popsicles and cool towels. The staff members were incredible - from helping with directions to caring for our every needs. The general manager was awesome and went over the top in making sure that we were satisfied. Would we stay there again? In a heartbeat. For us, the Magical Hotel was magical!

<Author>JAL25
<Content>Five Stars in Our Book!!! We have been traveling for over twenty years. Never have we encountered a staff like the crew employed by the Magic Castle Hotel. These young people go the extra mile to make your stay in Hollywood memorable. We returned from a month-long vacation of the West Coast having stayed in 22 hotels and the Magic Castle was without a doubt the best experience. I was leery booking a hotel for a week which AAA rated only two diamonds but after reading the reviews by the folks on Trip Advisor, I decided to ignore the pros. Wise choice. The hotel is in an excellent location for tourist yet quiet. We did not want to rent a car as my husband had already driven 1,200 miles on the first leg of the trip. This hotel is close to all forms of public transportation and sightseeing venues. We arrived three hours before check-in time in hopes of storing our luggage. To our shock, the staff said our room was ready and we had been given a complimentary upgrade to a suite!!! The suite was immaculate. The staff recommended which tours were worthwhile, what to see on our own and how to get there and advised us what we should NOT do via public transportation. I had wanted to take the transit system to Long Beach to tour the Queen Mary. They were adamant it would not be safe to do so. Only my mother has ever been this concerned for my well-being. The staff even went so far as to call taxi services on my behalf (without my asking) to check rates to Long Beach. They advised public transportation to The Reagan Library in one day was not do-able either....too many stops thus not enough time to tour the Library. The staff booked tours for us, which when we tried to book ourselves, were told there were no openings....hence the name Magic! The heated outdoor pool in the courtyard is open 24/7. They just ask you keep the noise level reasonable after 9pm. The on-site laundry facility is suppose to close at 9pm but when I was doing laundry after that hour, they said no problem. When I inquired as to why AAA only rated the hotel two diamonds, they explained that several factors are considered by AAA in their assessment which they don't tell the reader. 1. There is no bathroom in the lobby. This is silly as all 39 guestrooms are a short walk from the lobby. 2. There is no elevator. Another stupidity as there are only two floors. 3. No restaurant on site. Another no-brainer......there are two very classy restaurants right next door. The AAA rating of two diamonds is a terrible injustice to this wonderful hotel and their employees. To Ashley, Gretchen, Jason, Nick, Shawn and everyone else we came in contact with during the week......thank you.....you are all five stars in our book!!!!  
<Date>Aug 15, 2005

<Author>JulieAppleValley
<Content>A treasure, A+ My family and I just returned from a 6 night stay at the Magic Castle, July 23 - 29. On our last day at the hotel, as we were departing, I told the wonderful front office manager, Mike, that my only hesitation in writing a review on TripAdvisor, was that the hotel may be discovered. Mike assured me that he would always make room for me at their property. So, with that assurance, here's my review of the Magic Castle Hotel.What I loved most about the Magic Castle: it's quaint, it has character, it has charm, it has personality, and it's in a fabulous location (off the beaten path but close to the Hollywood strip). I also loved that it's in a safe location. The housekeeper even stopped up to our room a few times to see if my son was doing okay -- and offered him chocolates! The staff -- Ashley, Gretchen, and Shawn -- couldn't have been more helpful and polite. They *all* treated me like royalty, despite the thousands of questions I asked as I finagled LA and the metro bus system (I didn't rent a car but managed to get along just fine.) I couldn't take home their Egyptian robes, their goose down comforter or their nummy blueberry muffins -- but I could, and will, take home the memories of our delightful stay at the Magic Castle Hotel. I'll also take with me the wonderful memories of our last night's dinner at the spectacular Yamashiro restaurant, and the lasting memory of the Sunday branch and magic show at the exclusive Magic Castle club attached to the hotel. Also, I'll always remember how thrilled I was when I learned, as I was checking in, that they had upgraded our room! My kids were so excited too, especially when they saw the awesome huge rooms.This was a special trip for my two children and me. I booked my room nine months ago, and have been planning this vacation for nearly a year. Now that I'm back in Minnesota, I realize I couldn't have made a more perfect choice. All the glowing reviews on TripAdvisor are right on. Thank you to all the accommodating staff, and thank you once again to Mike, the front office manager. As I departed from the hotel, I gave Mike three hugs. That's something I must say I've never done before, but I was so happy with our stay; we all had such a great time on our vacation. Looking back, I wish I would have him yet another hug. Mike and all the staff at the Magic Castle deserve it!

<Author>Katoomba_Traveller
<Content>A great value Hollywood experience My wife and I stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel for 7 days as the last stop on a two month round the world trip. Our itinerary included a number of hotels in the $US150-$200 range across the globe and we would have to say that the Magic Castle was by far our best hotel experience. The friendliness of the staff is exceptional and extends way beyond the shallow have a nice day that often passes for good service in the US. The staff and management appeared genuinely eager to assist in any way to make our stay as enjoyable as possible - (well done guys!).The hotel itself is ideally located in the heart of the resurgent Hollywood district and for a tourist has that quintessential Hollywood feel. This was aided by the hotel's apparent appeal to out-of-town creative types who stay there for a day or two to pitch their film scripts - so wireless laptops and movie talk by the pool. The hotel is actually split in two, with the main building down the bottom of the hill and another one up the top. We initially booked a room up the hill and although the LA views are good, these rooms had not been renovated (Jan 2005) and were rundown. Guests are also required to walk up and down the hill for breakfast and any other concierge needs. After a couple of days, we decided to move into the main building and were put in a much nicer, larger and newly renovated room that was surprisingly at a lower price. The Magic Castle is not an international luxury business hotel (and hence lacks some of the trimmings), but is excellent value for those seeking an LA experience at a reasonable price. (Note we have also stayed at the similarly priced LAX Airport Sheraton, which is a good hotel too, but has no atmosphere)Some tips:To avoid disappointment, we suggest that you ask for an upstairs renovated room in the main building that faces the pool and is not on the main road.Guests at the Magic Castle Hotel are given the privilege of being able to visit the Magic Castle club next door to watch some of the top magicians in the world perform in a range of atmospheric theatres in a big Victorian house. Even if you stay for one night at the hotel, definitely take up this offer (and book ahead) as it is a genuinely unique LA experience that is not open to the general public. Visit the Japanese restaurant at the top of the hill (behind the hotel) for either dinner or a late night drink as it has some of the best views in LA. We were lucky enough to be there after heavy rain and the views were exceptional.  
<Date>Jul 27, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Magic Castle is the best! This hotel was so cool!I loved the vibe of the place, and if you're touring Hollywood this is the place to stay. You can walk to Hollywood Blvd, but the hotel is quiet and relaxing. I loved the retro feel, especially how rooms open onto the pool courtyard. You feel like Marilyn Monroe could be sunbathing there. Plus, there's a guy who comes around with complimentary popsicles :-)The rooms themselves are great. We stayed in the 2BR/2BA suite (myself and husband, and his parents) and had plenty of space. The full kitchen was a great way to not have to eat out every night, and it was great to eat breakfast in before heading out for the day. The beds were comfortable and there was a ton of closet space.One note: While the suite had window AC units, the bedroom my husband and I stayed in had a sub-par non-window AC. It didn't matter so much because the weather was perfect, but I wouldn't have been so happy in mid-July. However, the rest of the place was so nice it didn't really hurt our stay.The staff was extremely nice and very accommodating to our large number of suitcases and 4am departure time. We were in town for a family wedding at Yamshiro and it was so convenient to take Magic Castle's shuttle up to the restaurant. I will definitely be staying here next time I come to LA!

<Author>MDUK
<Content>Magic We found this hotel on trip advisor while we were looking for reviews of the Holiday Inn, the original hotel we were going to stay at. We decided to try 'The Magic' because of the reviews, its link with the adjoing magic club and were attracted by its general quirkiness.It is ideally situated for Hollywood boulevard, being less than 5 minutes walk away. We had a car (which we kept in the secure underground car park overnight for $8 a night) and drove to Disneyland which took around an hour and Universal studios which took about 10 minutes.The accomodation was ideal for a family, a double room and a bed setee in the lounge, basic kitchen facilities and seperate bathroom. The FREE buffet breakfast was well received by the children (cereal and croissants being much closer to their normal fayre than the heavy cooked buffets offerred elsewhere). Echoing previous reviews though, the hotel does need to invest in some more tables and chairs in that area.The staff are the one single differentiator from any of the other hotels we visited during our 2 weeks in the states. Without exception, they all try and make a difference to your stay. Really first class hospitality. Special mention to Gretchen and Jason.Would I stay again- definitely.

<Author>jacsbri
<Content>A Magical Experience From the moment I called the Magic Castle Hotel to make our reservations I encounter a friendly and caring of staff. I told the person at the other end of the line, my husband and I were celebrating our 40th Wedding Anniversary! That's FOUR DECADES, yikes! The young woman chuckled at my comment. I explained my husband is legally blind, and I am anticipating knee surgery within the near future. She said, No, problem. We have the perfect room for you. She was right! I asked her to please tell about the hotel ... describe it. She said the courtyard looks like a scene from the television program a few years ago called 'Melrose Place.' And that's exactly what we found ... we felt like we had walked into a movie set. The desk assistant that checked us in greeted us with a huge smile, helped me with our bags, explained some of the surround sites, and told us about the continental breakfast offered each morning. Our room was lovely. You could tell it was an older hotel that had been refurbished. But with great attention to detail! It was so clean. The bed was comfortable with a wonderful soft duvet. There was a refrigerator, a coffee maker, blow dryer, huge remote control television, makeup mirror, delicious smelling tangerine smelling soap, shampoo and cream rinse and abundance of wonderful fluffy towels. The staff surprised us with a small Anniversary cake and a card signed by each member of the staff. It was like having family help us celebrate! Additionally, the individual who made our hotel reservations, went one step further, and offered to make our dinner reservations at the Magic Castle Club for us as well. At the Club we received VIP treatment. If you are in the Hollywood area ... stay at the Magic Castle Hotel. We highly recommend it! Your stay will be magical!

<Author>stephanieOakton_VA
<Content>The Magic Castle is truly the "yes" hotel Where do you stay when your group consists of 38 high school drama students and chaperones coming to Hollywood for the first time from Virginia?? You want them to be welcomed, safe, comfortable and in a great location. The answer was a real winner....The Magic Castle Hotel!We all had suite rooms so the students felt more like they were in apartments rather than hotel rooms. The beds were all queen and king size so everyone was comfortable. The bedding is new, fresh and so comfortable you could melt into it. Each room had a kitchen, so the students could make snacks for themselves.Each morning a continental breakfast is provided, but not like at most places. The Magic Castle has fresh baked goods from a bakery and gourmet coffee. The juices and milk were quickly refilled, and the cereals and fruit bountiful. The morning we left at 5:00a.m. the hotel had an individual breakfast bag for each student as they boarded the bus!! How thoughtful can you be!?!?!?The location on this property is amazing. It is one block from the Kodak theater area. So it is in walking distance of many area attractions, shopping, restaurants, and the Metro. There was also a guard on the property to ensure safety, although we never felt unsafe.Because this hotel is associated with the Magic Castle itself any guest has the ability to go to this exclusive magic mecca. The Sunday brunch admits children and has shows that are age appropriate....and the buffet was out of this world. yum!The best part about the Magic Castle Hotel is the staff itself. They call themselves the yes hotel, and they live up to it. When we arrived they served popsicles! When the students needed anything they felt comfortable going to the front desk and asking for everything from paper/pen to milk for scrambling eggs. A lot of the front desk workers are young working actors and are happy to share their stories. Every single employee was a delight and so willing to be of service. Unselfish service is hard to find today, but the Magic Castle Hotel offers it bountifully.This hotel is a rare find, perfect for our group, and I hope others will enjoy it tool

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Not bad but somewhat disappointing I booked the Magic Castle Hotel on the basis of the reviews on this website and the fantastic photographs on the hotel's website. Only when we arrived did we realise that the photos on the website are mainly from the magic club, which is completely separate from the hotel annexe and quite different in style. The hotel part is small and set around a courtyard, there are lots of steps to navigate if you have heavy luggage or are unsteady on your feet and no elevator (check out the photos posted by another reviewer). The rooms are pretty basic and our bathroom was quite roughly finished, but it was clean and comfortable and had everything you need, including a refrigerator. The table top ironing board was a pain as it collapsed every time any kind of pressure was applied - a regular ironing board would have been much better. Other than that, the facilities in the room were fine and the shower was EXTREMELY powerful! It was quite noisy at night with other guests arriving back late and also there was some traffic noise as our room was right by a side street. Breakfast was OK. The big pluses for this hotel are its location, the reasonable cost and the extremely helpful and pleasant staff, especially Mike - give that man a raise! My overall impression was that this hotel was fine for the money but I am still confused by the fabulous reviews on this website - I've stayed in worse but I've stayed in better.

<Author>MardiGrasGourmet
<Content>Nice . . . . becoming GREAT! Just back from 3 nights in Hollywood March 19 - 22. This smallish hotel offers a fantastic location for seeing the sights on Hollywood Blvd. The Mann is one block down. Our room was a bit worn, RM 204. Older furnishings, some missing tile in the bath and the kids were not happy with the lumpy springs in the pullout. There is currently remodeling taking place, and the remodeled rooms are much nicer. A delightful staff more than made up what we lacked in our room. I have traveled to many places and have NEVER encountered people like the staff at this hotel. The Ritz cannot compare, and that is no BS. They made suggestions for tours, made reservations, attended to our requests, and even went out of their way on more than one occasion for us. Do yourself a favor and book a remodeled room and enjoy your time in Hollywood.

<Author>AmyKate222
<Content>Lived up to it's glowing recommendations!!!!!! My friend and I stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel for 1 night this past week. Honestly, I was skeptical... I mean, it was only a one star hotel, and the price seemed a little high for the rating. First off, when we drove up, we went to the club, not the hotel. The pictures on the web-site gave the impression that the club (which has a fantastic, victorian exterior) was the Hotel. So, when we tried to valet the car, we were sorely dissappointed when we were directed down the street. When we pulled up, we were unimpressed. Not dirty or anything, just plain. But when we entered the lobby, and then went to the courtyard, we were very impressed, especially with the multi-levels at the courtyard. Shawn, the guy who helped us, was SO NICE!!! Come to think of it, everyone we encountered at the hotel was incredibly pleasant, not in a fake way, but in a way that made you feel right at home.Since it was dark when we arrived, I was nervous about walking to downtown. Being from a small town, I asked Shawn if it was safe to walk the block to Hollywood Blvd. He assured us that it was, and that if we needed anything, to call him and he would have some one pick us up. He gave us a personalized map, a business card with numbers, a recommendation for dinner, and sent us on our merry way... Ok, now for the part that I guess is more relevant... The room... We got a small room with a king-sized bed. When we opened the door, the first impression was how great it smelled. I know that may sound odd, but it was a great, clean, fresh fragrence. The bed was SUPER comfy (pillow top) and the duvet was nice and fluffy. The bathroom was all new with a pedestal sink and cool track lighting. The plantation blinds were great at blocking out light too. The room itself was pretty small, but we were blown away with just how nice everything was in it (from the bed-side lamps, which doubled as night lights to the big tv).All in all, I would most definatly stay at the Magic Castle again. I would suggest that you book your stay while the rates are still low, because I think this place is going to continue to get better (they are renovating the rooms) and get a couple more stars :-)

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great service, great room, great location, great price! In general, I was very happy with my experience at the hotel. We stayed there for 5 nights, and we had no problems. This hotel is definitely one of the better places I've stayed. This was my first trip to Los Angeles. The people at the front desk were very friendly and helpful, giving us accurate directions to wherever we wanted to go.This building was an old apartment building, and it doesn't have any elevators. There are plenty of stairs to climb, so if you're physically disabled or have problems walking, this may not be the place for you. The rooms, however, are fantastic! If you get a suite (which I thought were reasonably priced), you will get a bedroom, a bathroom, a living room (with couch and coffee table, not to mention the DVD player and television), and a kitchen. The beds were very comfortable, and there are air conditioning units in the rooms.The Magic Castle Hotel has a private garage, which you will receive a key for when you receive your room key. I found this very comforting, as it is a small garage, and no one else has access to it besides the hotel guests.There is a nice pool at the center of the hotel, and also a continental breakfast every morning, which includes pastries, toast, cereal, fresh fruit, coffee, milk, and juices. It's not a large breakfast, but it's sufficient to get you through the day.Uphill from the hotel is the Magic Castle Club (you must be 21 to enter). It is located in a Victoria-era house, complete with some secret passageways and a piano-playing ghost. The club is exclusive, and you can only be allowed in by a member of the club or by making reservations at the front desk. I had a very good time going and watching the magic shows there. (There is a $15 cover charge, and you must order food... but the food is good, and the shows are worth it).As for location, the hotel is 2 blocks from Hollywood Blvd... we walked to the Walk of Fame and Grauman's Chinese theater. It is located near an entrance to Hwy 101, Sunset Blvd, and La Brea avenue, which will get you pretty much anywhere you want to go in and around Los Angeles.I hope that this review has been helpful to you... I would DEFINITELY RECOMMEND this hotel. :-)  
<Date>Mar 21, 2005
