<Author>Yankdo
<Content>Magic Castle What a Find! Just came back from a 4 night stay at Magic Castle Hotel - What a great stay! Everything about the hotel starting with my first call to book a room and get info was surprisingly pleasant. I can't say enough good things. Really! We arrived in the rain Feb 22 (umbrellas were provided in the lobby) and were given a first floor 1 bedroom apartment (they remembered that I had my 88 yr old Mom with me and I was travelling with my 11 yr old girl and 15 yr old son (a.k.a. The Bickersons) and needed plenty of room and 2 TV's! The room (really a 1 bedroom apt) was huge with so much storage space we couldn't use all the closets! Yes the apartment was older but ours was clean and everyone was so very nice and helpful that any wear and tear should just be considered shabby chic.The breakfast was great. The best croissants ever (Sat AM we had pain au chocolat better than Paris). We had the fortune/misfortune to be in Hollywood for the Oscars. The traffic was horrendous (Hollywood Blvd was blocked off due to security which made driving a challenge but the front desk staff helped me plot different routes to accommodate my mom visiting relatives by car. Most importantly for me as a woman travelling alone with kids and elderly person I felt very safe and completely at ease at this little gem of a hotel. Others have said it many times before but you just cannot beat the location of this hotel. It is close to all the touristy things and so easy to catch tours around town or do the funky museums around Hollywood Blvd. The Hollywood/Highland complex has lots of eating places and there are loads of places to go within walking distance. I am not sure if the staff reads these reports but a special thank you to Shawn at the front desk, I hope they pay you well because you really are an asset to Magic Castle!I could go on and on but I do want to say Thank you TripAdvisor because the Magic Castle really made our trip enjoyable and I really would never have picked it out randomly without all the great truthful reports.

<Author>lass=
<Content>Great Location! I chose this hotel based on three things: location, access to the Magic Castle Club and TripAdvisor reviews. Keep in mind this is not a luxury hotel. Never mind the Wolfgang Puck coffee and Bath Bloomers toiletries. As its rating suggests, this is not a luxury hotel. However, the staff is very friendly and attentive and you can't beat the great location. As noted in previous user reviews, it is walking distance to many Hollywood attractions and the Metro. Unfortunately, the rain prevented us from seeing/using the hotel to its best advantage. Given the weather, we chose not to swim or use our balcony although other guests did. We were given a one-bedroom suite in the back on the third floor which appears not to have been redone. While the decor was tired, we appreciated the space, spending more time inside than we had anticipated due to the rain. Ask for another room if you cannot climb stairs. Everyone raves about the continental breakfast, which I would rate as average. Again because of the rain, we were unable to eat outside next the the pool (which ended up almost overflowing and had to be drained at the end of the weekend) and had to carefully make our way back to the room balancing our trays while climbing two flights of stairs. Staying at the hotel would have been easier in sunny, dry weather! The bottom line is that if you are looking for a hotel room under $200 with lots of space in a great location this is the hotel for you.  
<Date>Feb 24, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Magic Castle is the place to stay I did lots of research before booking accomodation in LA, and based on what I had read on the reviews here, decided to base myself at the Magic Castle Hotel. The hotel did not disappoint. The location, for starters is hard to beat. The hotel itself - the size of the suite is just amazing, it was much more like living in an apartment then in a hotel room. There was a kitchen (complete with oven, microwave, full sized fridge, cutlery), dining table, pull out sofa, bath room, bedroom and the overall living room space was very spacious. The breakfast every morning was great, an assortments of cereals, pasteries, drinks and fruits that you can eat out by the patio area near the pool or take back to your room.The staff were also top-notch. Friendly, and always willing to answer questions at any time or provide assistance, they know how to deliver the best customer service!Lastly, if you don't have a laptop to make use of the wireless internet connection at the hotel, there is also an Internet kiosk available for use at the hotel.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Exceptional Service My husband and I and our three children stayed at the Magic Castle from December 30-January 2, 2005. We had a one bedroom suite and found it to be old, but clean with lots of pillows and fluffy comforters. I loved having the use of the guest laundry and one of the front desk folks even went so far as to go home in a rain storm and bring back dryer sheets when I asked if they had any available for purchase! The pool was located in a nice courtyard. We didn't get to use it because of the rain and the temperature, but it looked clean and inviting. The continental breakfast served in the lobby was very nice. The coffee was very good (I heard someone say it was Wolfgang Puck coffee) and the pastries and breads were fresh. They also had some fresh fruit (apples and tangerines) and a good assortment of juices, tea and hot chocolate. The location of the hotel is great. It is located on a quiet street off of Hollywood Blvd. It has easy access to the Metro station as well as major freeways. I would definitely recommend this hotel.

<Content>Loved the Magic Castle We stayed at the Magic Castle from December 25 to 27, and couldn't have been happier. We were immediately upgraded to a one bedroom suite, my sister was upgraded to a 2 bedroom suite. Whilst the rooms are certainly basic, they have everything you need and are quite comfortable, with very comfortable beds. The hotel was originally an apartment building, and retains that homely feel. The staff could not have been more helpful, answering any of our questions and assisting wherever possible. The breakfast in the lobby was simple, but ample, and each evening there was hot cider and cookies in the lobby. The location is perfect, you feel like you are in a suburban oasis, yet 2 minutes walk down the street and you are in the heart of Hollywood. It is close to transport, shops and restaurants.Overall, if you want something fancy, don't stay here. However if you want a comfortable hotel, with exceptionally friendly staff in an excellent location, this is the place for you. We would definitely stay there again.

<Author>cambriant
<Content>Great Location but average hotel room... We stayed at Magic Castle from 21-26th December. First of all, I must say that the hotel was really conveniently located to most of all the attractions. Barely 1 block from Hollywood Boulevard, 5 minutes drive from Universal Studio, 15-20 min drive to downtown and close to Getty Center. Since it was our first time in LA, and I'm usually not too good with car rides, it was really great that everything was close in proximity. The hotel room was alright. It was clean, but the house cleaning wasn't too thorough. Shampoo supplies were never replenished during the 5 night stay we were there. Cups that we used to make hot drinks were never washed. The room wasn't the newest, but it was clean. Not that big, but considering the terrific location, it was great. If you are planning on staying at the Magic Castle, I would strongly recommend spending an additional $20 for a one bedroom apartment. I caught a glimpse of the apartment from time to time, and it seemed so much newer and spacious, and more inviting. We were trying to save some money, but kinda wished we had spent that additional $20/night. Apart from that, hotel staff were really friendly and helpful. Continental Breakfast (Croissants, muffins, scones, toast from a local bakery) is actually self service, available in the small lobby. I love the croissants, but they seem to run out pretty early in the morning. But all in all, it was a great stay. I would stay there again, for the excellent location, but would definitely fork out the extra money to get a one bedroom apartment.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>MCH and Hollywood Hills Hollywood Hills Hotel  Magic Castle Hotel are run by the same people. Walking distance to Mann's Chinese and Hollywood Blvd. Walk of Fame. Check-in at MCH lobby. Gated parking is $8. The HHH is at the top of the hill, across from Yamashiro Japanese restaurant. MCH at bottom of hill, across from the famous Magic Castle. Great views on top at HHH; there's a big, quiet pool up there too but it needs a new pool floor. MCH pool is much smaller  less private but newer/better maintained.My first room at HHH had a fantastic view but carpet and chairs were worn and stained. I asked to be moved to one of the newly refurbished rooms (improvement going on at both HHH  MCH). The staff was very understanding and immediately moved me to a new suite at the same price. Nice staff here, unlike some other uptight LA places.Continental breakfast served in MC lobby is great, but somewhat incovenient for HHH guests who must walk or drive down the hill. Not enough seating too.If you stay at either HHH or MCH, you get access to the Magic Castle next door, an extremely cool private club of magicians. Plan a night for dinner there-- wander around the club afterwards, it's awesome. Jacket/tie required for men.I'll be back!

<Author>au175
<Content>Good hotel I initially stayed at this hotel 4 years ago and it was very impressive. I recently just come back from LA and stayed at Magic for 3 days and it was pleasant. It is now under new management and the reception area has been totally redone and it looks very nice.The swimming pool is brilliant, good size and clean. It is always quiet and you can enjoy a daily swim with the pool all to yourself. However the rooms are a bit dated and the furniture is in need of replacement but for the price you cannot complain. As for the previous review about the parking being $8 a day, this is totally untrue. Parking is free for all guests and you are given a key to open the electronic gate into the underground garage.All attractions are nearby. Hollywood walk of fame is a 5 minute walk and universal city is a 10 minute drive. For night life, the sunset strip is a 15 minute drive and must be checked out. And as for Santa Monica Beach  Venice Beach, these are about 30 40 minute drive from the hotel. This hotel is the perfect location for someone wanting to explore LA. <Author>Graysgirl
<Content>Excellent value, lovely staff Our family stayed in one of the two bedroomed suites with efficiencies earlier this month, and were delighted. It is very good value, near to all the Hollywood sights (2 minutes walk), but away from the noise and bustle. We cannot speak highly enough of the staff, who are delightful and who provide 5 star service in a 2 star rated hotel - bed turndown with chocs, loads of white towels appearing at the pool, lots of helpful suggestions on things to do and places to eat; the continental breakfast with amazing pastries and the sheer space of the suite; also plentiful secure underground parking at $8 a day. The hotel is in the course of renovation, as other Tripadvisor reviewers have noted, so during the day the hotel can be noisy, and our suite was in need of its update - but was pleasant and clean - much nicer than some well known chains. Also the pool is not heated. Overall we all agreed this has been the nicest place we have stayed in as a family for many years.

<Author>DMK0908
<Content>Decent hotel, great location We stayed at the Magic Castle a few weeks ago. First, I have to say it's in a GREAT location if you're a tourist. It's a block from the Chinese theater  Kodak theater, and also very close to restaurants, shopping, the Hollywood Bowl, etc. We were able to walk nearly everywhere we wanted to go, including to the tour we signed up for (recommended by the hotel). We were really happy with the location. As for the room, it was so much smaller than we expected! I guess this wasn't one of the refurbished rooms they show on the website? We didn't complain because we didn't plan on spending much time in the room. In fact, we didn't even get to use the pool (or sit out by the pool) because we were so busy. There were some families out by the pool who seemed to be enjoying themselves--it was a pleasant atmosphere. One great feature was that we were able to take our breakfast back to the room on a tray, so we could eat while planning our day. I would have liked more room to spread out (we had a lot of luggage, and kept tripping over our suitcases!), but that was my main complaint. The bathroom only had a small shower stall, but on the bright side they have really nice smelling soaps and shampoos! There is a nightly turndown service and they bring you clean towels and leave a chocolate on your pillow. I thought that was a nice touch. The staff was really helpful in answering our questions and suggesting tours. Everyone was really friendly, which helped to make our stay pleasant. We did eat dinner at Yamashiro restaurant one night, and while the food was good, you're paying for the view more than anything. You can get equally good Japanese food at less expensive restaurants. I would recommend this hotel if you're on a budget or traveling with children and want a hotel close to all the Hollywood attractions.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Pay extra for the suite My wife and I spent a week here in June 2004. We originally booked a 'single' room for $99 p/n, but when we arrived we weren't happy with it. The furniture was old, the room overlooked the car park, and the bathroom wasn't particularly clean. We asked to look at one of the suites, and the difference was amazing. We instantly upgraded - OK, the price went up to $159 p/n, but it was definitely worth it. We had a big lounge/kitchen with oven, microwave, coffee machine etc, plus a much grander bedroom and bathroom and a front-facing balcony.The location is perfect for sightseeing - you can walk down to Hollywood or Sunset in minutes or quickly get on a road to the beach if you're driving.Parking is now $8 per day.Staff friendly and helpful, and there's also a nice (but small) pool in the centre of the facility.

<Content>Disappointed with our stay. We were not happy with our stay at the Magic Castle. When I booked the room, I requested a refurbished room. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Reasonable but in need of refurbishment! Stayed here for 3 nights in a 2 bedroom suite (2 king beds and 1 queen sofa bed). Having read the reviews on this site I decided to stay at the Magic Castle. However, given the reviews, the price and the other hotels I have stayed at on this trip I was pretty disappointed! First the negatives: phone and safe in my room did not work (although I was offered a new suite, but didn't take due to the large amount of lugguage we had. Instead, we got a discount on our room rate, which I thought was pretty good of them), there is no air conditioning in the bedrooms (fans only, although there is air conditioning in the living room), air conditioning in the living room is really really loud - can't sleep with it on, the room was really old - they definitely need some new furniture and the suite was really noisy (noise from other room's ac, all doors in the hotel slam - not good if you are not an early riser, noise from above apartment, noisey plumming. I did not sleep that well during my stay at the Magic Castle). Also the price is pretty expensive. However, there are a number of offsetting positives: great breakfast, staff are really helpful, parking is cheap (note there is now $8 parking charge per night), big suites, good kitchen, great location (very close to Hollywood Bl, also close to Freeway 101  Griffith park). On balance, would stay here again but would not be my first choice. This place is good for families or large groups.

<Author>termoo
<Content>nice, homey place 4/12/04 - 4/14/04My 10-year-old daughter and I stayed here on a trip to Hollywood. The location was great--we could easily walk the couple of blocks down to Hollywood Blvd., Chinese Theatre, Hollywood  Highland Shopping District, etc. The hotel suite was nice--nothing too fancy, but not ratty either--but smelled like smoke. I called down to the front desk and they said all of their rooms were non-smoking. I asked why there was an ashtray on the kitchen table and he seemed surprised. I guess other guests must have smoked out on the balcony with the doors open. He offered to move us to a different room, but since the other room had not been recently renovated like ours had, we opted for airing it out. We left the windows open (nice that they OPENED!) for the rest of the day and that helped a lot. We had a TON of space with a separate bedroom with a huge closet, a living room area with a hide-a-bed and another closet, and a dining area and full kitchen, as well as a large, nicely appointed bathroom. There was a balcony that faced out onto Franklin Ave. I'd recommend asking for a room that has a balcony overlooking the pool instead. Everything was very clean, and all of the employees were extremely friendly. I liked the fact that the hotel used to be an apartment building--it gave it more of a homey feel than most hotels. The swimming pool was very warm, but there was no hot tub. Parking is underground in a locked garage; it's pretty small, so it was tricky maneuvering our car down there. However, we rarely used the car, so that wasn't a problem. Breakfast was homemade croissants, muffins and scones from a local bakery, as well as cereal, toast, danish, fruit juices, coffee, tea and milk. The tables are set up around the pool area. This is a great place for families, since you have a full kitchen and lots of space. I'd go back again!  
<Date>May 5, 2004

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Good value and view We recently stayed at the Magic Castle Hotel based solely on the TripAdvisor.com reviews. While I was pleased with the hotel itself, it wasn't exactly what I expected. We stayed in the Hollywood Hills portion of the hotel. The set-up was unconventional - several sections of what seemed like short-term apartments. The view was great with a nice balcony; however, it was generally foggy/smoggy, so we couldn't see terribly far. It was nice to walk to the Hollywood attractions, though it was a bit tough trekking up and down the steep hill with two small children in a stroller. But good exercise! And watch out for the traffic on the hill at night going to and from the Japanese restaurant at the top. From the hotel's website, it looks very secluded, but it's right off the side of a busy street. The continental breakfast was great with freshly baked muffins and scones from a local bakery. I think my experience at the hotel may have been a bit tainted by the fact that Hollywood generally isn't my favorite place, particularly with two small children.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Clean  My husband and I spent 5 nights at the Magic Castle Hotel last week and we highly recommend it to anyone going to L.A. It's close to Hollywood  Highland, but it also wasn't a bad drive to the valley where our son lives. Our room was a single with a queen bed, dresser, tv, desk 2 nightstands and large closet with plenty of hangers for once. It was small, but how much room do you need? The front desk staff was excellent and couldn't have been nicer. The continental breakfast was ok. Cereal, muffins, apples and oranges, juices, coffee, tea, etc. Nothing special, but very nice and the muffins were tasty. The rooms are arranged around a lovely courtyard pool--think Melrose Place--as this was once an apartment building. The parking garage is small but we had no problems finding a space at various times a day. On days when we would be sight-seeing nearer our hotel than our son's apartment, they even let our son drive over and park in our space while we were out in the rental car. Our only problem was the maid. For some reason, she missed giving us wash cloths on 3 days. We got towels, but only one washcloth, and one day none! My husband had to go down to the desk to get them. But other than that minor inconvenience, everything was excellent and we would definitely stay there again. One other thing is the walls are a little thin and we could hear a family with a crying baby on the other side of ours. Our son had gone to check the place out before we booked, and he asked them to give us a room away from the street because he was afraid it would be too noisy. I'm not sure it would have been, but it was quiet except for the baby and that didn't really bother us. All in all, a very good hotel for the money. Our AAA rate was $89.10 a night, plus tax for a total of $507.85 for 5 nights. Also, as someone else said already, be sure to drive up to the Japanese restaurant on the hill behind the hotel. It's a beautiful view and it's just a pretty place. My husband hiked up there one morning for exercise. It's a bit pricey to eat there, and I don't care for sushi, so we didn't consider it, but it's lovely. We were up there around 10 pm and the valet let us park for a few minutes and look around. So don't be afraid to book a room at the Magic Castle. You'll be happy you did.
